# 2. src/config.py
import os
from typing import Optional
from pydantic_settings import BaseSettings
from pydantic import PostgresDsn, validator


class Settings(BaseSettings):
    # App
    APP_NAME: str = "DIYAPP V10 Core"
    APP_VERSION: str = "1.0.0"
    DEBUG: bool = False
    
    # Security
    SECRET_KEY: str = "your-secret-key-change-in-production"
    ALGORITHM: str = "HS256"
    ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES: int = 30
    REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS: int = 7
    
    # Database
    DATABASE_URL: Optional[str] = None
    DATABASE_TEST_URL: str = "sqlite:///./test.db"
    
    @validator("DATABASE_URL", pre=True)
    def assemble_db_connection(cls, v: Optional[str], values: dict) -> str:
        if isinstance(v, str):
            return v
        
        # Use SQLite for development, PostgreSQL for production
        if os.getenv("ENVIRONMENT") == "production":
            return PostgresDsn.build(
                scheme="postgresql",
                user=os.getenv("POSTGRES_USER", "diyapp"),
                password=os.getenv("POSTGRES_PASSWORD", ""),
                host=os.getenv("POSTGRES_HOST", "localhost"),
                port=os.getenv("POSTGRES_PORT", "5432"),
                path=f"/{os.getenv('POSTGRES_DB', 'diyapp')}",
            )
        else:
            return "sqlite:///./diyapp.db"
    
    # Redis for rate limiting and caching
    REDIS_URL: str = "redis://localhost:6379/0"
    
    # External services (with circuit breaker defaults)
    EXTERNAL_SERVICE_TIMEOUT: int = 5  # seconds
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURE_THRESHOLD: int = 5
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT: int = 60
    
    # Logging
    LOG_LEVEL: str = "INFO"
    
    class Config:
        env_file = ".env"
        case_sensitive = True


settings = Settings()

# 3. src/database/connection.py
from sqlalchemy import create_engine
from sqlalchemy.ext.declarative import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker, Session
from contextlib import contextmanager
import structlog
from typing import Generator
from ..config import settings

logger = structlog.get_logger(__name__)

# Create engine with connection pooling
engine = create_engine(
    settings.DATABASE_URL,
    pool_pre_ping=True,  # Verify connections before using
    pool_recycle=3600,   # Recycle connections after 1 hour
    connect_args={"check_same_thread": False} if "sqlite" in settings.DATABASE_URL else {}
)

SessionLocal = sessionmaker(autocommit=False, autoflush=False, bind=engine)
Base = declarative_base()


@contextmanager
def get_db() -> Generator[Session, None, None]:
    """Database session context manager with proper error handling."""
    db = SessionLocal()
    correlation_id = structlog.contextvars.get_contextvars().get("correlation_id", "unknown")
    
    try:
        logger.debug("database.session_started", correlation_id=correlation_id)
        yield db
        db.commit()
        logger.debug("database.session_committed", correlation_id=correlation_id)
    except Exception as e:
        db.rollback()
        logger.error(
            "database.session_rollback",
            correlation_id=correlation_id,
            error=str(e),
            error_type=type(e).__name__
        )
        raise
    finally:
        db.close()
        logger.debug("database.session_closed", correlation_id=correlation_id)


def init_db():
    """Initialize database tables."""
    Base.metadata.create_all(bind=engine)
    logger.info("database.initialized")

# 4. src/models/user.py
from sqlalchemy import Column, Integer, String, Boolean, DateTime, Text
from sqlalchemy.sql import func
from ..database.connection import Base
import uuid


class User(Base):
    __tablename__ = "users"
    
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)
    uuid = Column(String(36), unique=True, index=True, default=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
    email = Column(String(255), unique=True, index=True, nullable=False)
    username = Column(String(50), unique=True, index=True, nullable=False)
    hashed_password = Column(String(255), nullable=False)
    full_name = Column(String(100))
    is_active = Column(Boolean, default=True)
    is_superuser = Column(Boolean, default=False)
    created_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now())
    updated_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), onupdate=func.now())
    
    # Audit fields
    last_login = Column(DateTime(timezone=True))
    failed_login_attempts = Column(Integer, default=0)
    
    def to_dict(self, mask_sensitive: bool = True):
        """Convert to dict with sensitive data masking."""
        data = {
            "id": self.id,
            "uuid": self.uuid,
            "email": self.email if not mask_sensitive else self._mask_email(self.email),
            "username": self.username,
            "full_name": self.full_name,
            "is_active": self.is_active,
            "created_at": self.created_at.isoformat() if self.created_at else None,
            "updated_at": self.updated_at.isoformat() if self.updated_at else None,
        }
        return data
    
    @staticmethod
    def _mask_email(email: str) -> str:
        """Mask email for logging."""
        if "@" in email:
            local, domain = email.split("@")
            if len(local) > 2:
                masked = local[:2] + "*" * (len(local) - 2)
            else:
                masked = "**"
            return f"{masked}@{domain}"
        return "***@***"

# 5. src/models/project.py
from sqlalchemy import Column, Integer, String, Text, DateTime, ForeignKey, JSON
from sqlalchemy.orm import relationship
from sqlalchemy.sql import func
from ..database.connection import Base
import uuid


class Project(Base):
    __tablename__ = "projects"
    
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)
    uuid = Column(String(36), unique=True, index=True, default=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
    name = Column(String(200), nullable=False)
    description = Column(Text)
    status = Column(String(50), default="active")  # active, archived, deleted
    metadata = Column(JSON, default=dict)
    
    # Foreign keys
    owner_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("users.id"), nullable=False)
    
    # Timestamps
    created_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now())
    updated_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), onupdate=func.now())
    
    # Relationships
    owner = relationship("User")
    
    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            "id": self.id,
            "uuid": self.uuid,
            "name": self.name,
            "description": self.description,
            "status": self.status,
            "metadata": self.metadata,
            "owner_id": self.owner_id,
            "created_at": self.created_at.isoformat() if self.created_at else None,
            "updated_at": self.updated_at.isoformat() if self.updated_at else None,
        }

# 6. src/repositories/base.py
from typing import TypeVar, Type, Generic, List, Optional, Dict, Any
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from sqlalchemy import asc, desc
import structlog
from ..database.connection import Base as ModelBase

ModelType = TypeVar("ModelType", bound=ModelBase)
logger = structlog.get_logger(__name__)


class BaseRepository(Generic[ModelType]):
    def __init__(self, model: Type[ModelType], db: Session):
        self.model = model
        self.db = db
    
    def get(self, id: int) -> Optional[ModelType]:
        """Get by ID with parameterized query."""
        try:
            # Parameterized query - NO string concatenation
            return self.db.query(self.model).filter(self.model.id == id).first()
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(
                "repository.get_failed",
                model=self.model.__name__,
                id=id,
                error=str(e)
            )
            raise
    
    def get_by_uuid(self, uuid: str) -> Optional[ModelType]:
        """Get by UUID with parameterized query."""
        try:
            return self.db.query(self.model).filter(self.model.uuid == uuid).first()
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(
                "repository.get_by_uuid_failed",
                model=self.model.__name__,
                uuid=uuid,
                error=str(e)
            )
            raise
    
    def get_multi(
        self,
        skip: int = 0,
        limit: int = 100,
        filters: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
        order_by: Optional[str] = None,
        order_desc: bool = False
    ) -> List[ModelType]:
        """Get multiple records with filtering and pagination."""
        try:
            query = self.db.query(self.model)
            
            # Apply filters
            if filters:
                for field, value in filters.items():
                    if hasattr(self.model, field):
                        query = query.filter(getattr(self.model, field) == value)
            
            # Apply ordering
            if order_by and hasattr(self.model, order_by):
                if order_desc:
                    query = query.order_by(desc(getattr(self.model, order_by)))
                else:
                    query = query.order_by(asc(getattr(self.model, order_by)))
            
            # Apply pagination
            return query.offset(skip).limit(limit).all()
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(
                "repository.get_multi_failed",
                model=self.model.__name__,
                skip=skip,
                limit=limit,
                error=str(e)
            )
            raise
    
    def create(self, obj_in: Dict[str, Any]) -> ModelType:
        """Create new record."""
        try:
            db_obj = self.model(**obj_in)
            self.db.add(db_obj)
            self.db.flush()
            return db_obj
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(
                "repository.create_failed",
                model=self.model.__name__,
                error=str(e)
            )
            raise
    
    def update(self, db_obj: ModelType, obj_in: Dict[str, Any]) -> ModelType:
        """Update existing record."""
        try:
            for field, value in obj_in.items():
                if hasattr(db_obj, field):
                    setattr(db_obj, field, value)
            self.db.add(db_obj)
            self.db.flush()
            return db_obj
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(
                "repository.update_failed",
                model=self.model.__name__,
                obj_id=db_obj.id,
                error=str(e)
            )
            raise
    
    def delete(self, id: int) -> bool:
        """Delete record by ID."""
        try:
            obj = self.get(id)
            if obj:
                self.db.delete(obj)
                self.db.flush()
                return True
            return False
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(
                "repository.delete_failed",
                model=self.model.__name__,
                id=id,
                error=str(e)
            )
            raise

# 7. src/repositories/user_repository.py
from .base import BaseRepository
from ..models.user import User
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from typing import Optional


class UserRepository(BaseRepository[User]):
    def __init__(self, db: Session):
        super().__init__(User, db)
    
    def get_by_email(self, email: str) -> Optional[User]:
        """Get user by email with parameterized query."""
        return self.db.query(User).filter(User.email == email).first()
    
    def get_by_username(self, username: str) -> Optional[User]:
        """Get user by username with parameterized query."""
        return self.db.query(User).filter(User.username == username).first()
    
    def increment_failed_login(self, user_id: int) -> None:
        """Increment failed login attempts."""
        user = self.get(user_id)
        if user:
            user.failed_login_attempts = (user.failed_login_attempts or 0) + 1
            self.db.add(user)
            self.db.flush()
    
    def reset_failed_login(self, user_id: int) -> None:
        """Reset failed login attempts."""
        user = self.get(user_id)
        if user:
            user.failed_login_attempts = 0
            self.db.add(user)
            self.db.flush()

# 8. src/repositories/project_repository.py
from .base import BaseRepository
from ..models.project import Project
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from typing import List, Optional


class ProjectRepository(BaseRepository[Project]):
    def __init__(self, db: Session):
        super().__init__(Project, db)
    
    def get_by_owner(self, owner_id: int, skip: int = 0, limit: int = 100) -> List[Project]:
        """Get projects by owner ID."""
        return (
            self.db.query(Project)
            .filter(Project.owner_id == owner_id)
            .filter(Project.status != "deleted")
            .offset(skip)
            .limit(limit)
            .all()
        )
    
    def search(self, query: str, owner_id: Optional[int] = None) -> List[Project]:
        """Search projects by name or description."""
        search_query = (
            self.db.query(Project)
            .filter(Project.status != "deleted")
            .filter(
                (Project.name.ilike(f"%{query}%")) |
                (Project.description.ilike(f"%{query}%"))
            )
        )
        
        if owner_id:
            search_query = search_query.filter(Project.owner_id == owner_id)
        
        return search_query.all()

# 9. src/utils/security.py
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
from jose import JWTError, jwt
from passlib.context import CryptContext
import structlog
from ..config import settings

logger = structlog.get_logger(__name__)

pwd_context = CryptContext(schemes=["bcrypt"], deprecated="auto")


def verify_password(plain_password: str, hashed_password: str) -> bool:
    """Verify password against hash."""
    try:
        return pwd_context.verify(plain_password, hashed_password)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error("security.password_verification_failed", error=str(e))
        return False


def get_password_hash(password: str) -> str:
    """Generate password hash."""
    return pwd_context.hash(password)


def

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Containerização e Monitoramento

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10-core/
├── docker-compose.yml
├── Dockerfile
├── .env.example
├── docker/
│   ├── nginx/
│   │   └── nginx.conf
│   └── prometheus/
│       └── prometheus.yml
├── scripts/
│   ├── health-check.sh
│   ├── deploy.sh
│   └── backup.sh
├── src/
│   └── health/
│       └── health.js
└── README.md
```

## 1. Dockerfile

```dockerfile
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core
# Multi-stage build para otimização

# Stage 1: Build
FROM node:18-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

# Instala dependências de build
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copia código fonte
COPY . .

# Stage 2: Runtime
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# Instala dependências de runtime
RUN apk add --no-cache curl tini

# Copia node_modules e código do builder
COPY --from=builder /app/node_modules ./node_modules
COPY --from=builder /app/package*.json ./
COPY --from=builder /app/src ./src
COPY --from=builder /app/scripts ./scripts

# Cria usuário não-root para segurança
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs && \
    adduser -S nodejs -u 1001 && \
    chown -R nodejs:nodejs /app

USER nodejs

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
    CMD curl -f http://localhost:3000/health || exit 1

# Expose port
EXPOSE 3000

# Entry point
ENTRYPOINT ["/sbin/tini", "--"]
CMD ["node", "src/index.js"]
```

## 2. docker-compose.yml

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Aplicação principal
  app:
    build: .
    container_name: diyapp-v10-core
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - PORT=3000
      - LOG_LEVEL=info
    env_file:
      - .env
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs
      - ./data:/app/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 3s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 10s
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "10m"
        max-file: "3"

  # Nginx como reverse proxy e load balancer
  nginx:
    image: nginx:alpine
    container_name: diyapp-nginx
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "80:80"
      - "443:443"
    volumes:
      - ./docker/nginx/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
      - ./ssl:/etc/nginx/ssl:ro
    depends_on:
      - app
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "nginx", "-t"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 3s
      retries: 3

  # Prometheus para monitoramento
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    container_name: diyapp-prometheus
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    volumes:
      - ./docker/prometheus/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml:ro
      - prometheus_data:/prometheus
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries'
      - '--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/consoles'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=200h'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Node Exporter para métricas do sistema
  node-exporter:
    image: prom/node-exporter:latest
    container_name: diyapp-node-exporter
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "9100:9100"
    volumes:
      - /proc:/host/proc:ro
      - /sys:/host/sys:ro
      - /:/rootfs:ro
    command:
      - '--path.procfs=/host/proc'
      - '--path.rootfs=/rootfs'
      - '--path.sysfs=/host/sys'
      - '--collector.filesystem.mount-points-exclude=^/(sys|proc|dev|host|etc)($$|/)'
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # cAdvisor para métricas de containers
  cadvisor:
    image: gcr.io/cadvisor/cadvisor:latest
    container_name: diyapp-cadvisor
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    volumes:
      - /:/rootfs:ro
      - /var/run:/var/run:ro
      - /sys:/sys:ro
      - /var/lib/docker/:/var/lib/docker:ro
      - /dev/disk/:/dev/disk:ro
    privileged: true
    devices:
      - /dev/kmsg
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Grafana para dashboards
  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    container_name: diyapp-grafana
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=${GRAFANA_PASSWORD:-admin}
      - GF_INSTALL_PLUGINS=grafana-piechart-panel
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./grafana/dashboards:/etc/grafana/provisioning/dashboards
      - ./grafana/datasources:/etc/grafana/provisioning/datasources
    depends_on:
      - prometheus
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Redis para cache e sessões
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes --requirepass ${REDIS_PASSWORD:-redispass}
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "--raw", "incr", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 3s
      retries: 3

  # PostgreSQL para dados persistentes
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-postgres
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_USER=${DB_USER:-diyapp}
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${DB_PASSWORD:-diyapp123}
      - POSTGRES_DB=${DB_NAME:-diyapp_db}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./init.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U ${DB_USER:-diyapp}"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

volumes:
  prometheus_data:
  grafana_data:
  redis_data:
  postgres_data:

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge
    ipam:
      config:
        - subnet: 172.20.0.0/16
```

## 3. Configuração Nginx

`docker/nginx/nginx.conf`:
```nginx
events {
    worker_connections 1024;
}

http {
    upstream app_servers {
        server app:3000;
        # Adicionar mais instâncias para scaling
        # server app2:3000;
        # server app3:3000;
    }

    # Configuração de logging
    log_format main '$remote_addr - $remote_user [$time_local] "$request" '
                    '$status $body_bytes_sent "$http_referer" '
                    '"$http_user_agent" "$http_x_forwarded_for" '
                    'rt=$request_time uct="$upstream_connect_time" '
                    'uht="$upstream_header_time" urt="$upstream_response_time"';

    access_log /var/log/nginx/access.log main;
    error_log /var/log/nginx/error.log warn;

    # Configurações de segurança
    server_tokens off;
    client_max_body_size 10M;

    # Timeouts
    client_body_timeout 12;
    client_header_timeout 12;
    keepalive_timeout 15;
    send_timeout 10;

    # Gzip
    gzip on;
    gzip_vary on;
    gzip_min_length 1024;
    gzip_types text/plain text/css text/xml text/javascript application/javascript application/xml+rss application/json;

    server {
        listen 80;
        server_name localhost;

        # Health check endpoint
        location /health {
            proxy_pass http://app_servers/health;
            proxy_set_header Host $host;
            proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
            access_log off;
        }

        # Métricas do Prometheus
        location /metrics {
            proxy_pass http://prometheus:9090;
            auth_basic "Prometheus";
            auth_basic_user_file /etc/nginx/.htpasswd;
        }

        # Aplicação principal
        location / {
            proxy_pass http://app_servers;
            proxy_set_header Host $host;
            proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
            proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
            proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
            
            # Timeouts
            proxy_connect_timeout 5s;
            proxy_send_timeout 10s;
            proxy_read_timeout 10s;
            
            # Buffering
            proxy_buffering off;
            proxy_request_buffering off;
        }

        # Status do Nginx
        location /nginx_status {
            stub_status;
            access_log off;
            allow 127.0.0.1;
            allow 172.20.0.0/16;
            deny all;
        }
    }
}
```

## 5. Endpoint de Health Check

`src/health/health.js`:
```javascript
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const redis = require('redis');

// Configurações
const dbConfig = {
  user: process.env.DB_USER || 'diyapp',
  host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'postgres',
  database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp_db',
  password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD || 'diyapp123',
  port: process.env.DB_PORT || 5432,
};

const redisConfig = {
  url: `redis://:${process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD || 'redispass'}@redis:6379`
};

// Health check completo
router.get('/', async (req, res) => {
  const healthCheck = {
    status: 'healthy',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    checks: {
      app: { status: 'healthy', timestamp: new Date().toISOString() },
      database: { status: 'unchecked', latency: 0 },
      redis: { status: 'unchecked', latency: 0 },
      memory: { status: 'healthy', usage: process.memoryUsage() },
      uptime: process.uptime()
    }
  };

  try {
    // Check PostgreSQL
    const dbStart = Date.now();
    const dbPool = new Pool(dbConfig);
    const dbClient = await dbPool.connect();
    await dbClient.query('SELECT 1');
    dbClient.release();
    await dbPool.end();
    
    const dbLatency = Date.now() - dbStart;
    healthCheck.checks.database = {
      status: 'healthy',
      latency: dbLatency,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    };

    // Check Redis
    const redisStart = Date.now();
    const redisClient = redis.createClient(redisConfig);
    await redisClient.connect();
    await redisClient.ping();
    await redisClient.quit();
    
    const redisLatency = Date.now() - redisStart;
    healthCheck.checks.redis = {
      status: 'healthy',
      latency: redisLatency,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    };

  } catch (error) {
    healthCheck.status = 'unhealthy';
    
    if (error.code === 'ECONNREFUSED') {
      if (error.address === 'postgres') {
        healthCheck.checks.database = {
          status: 'unhealthy',
          error: 'Database connection refused',
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        };
      } else if (error.address === 'redis') {
        healthCheck.checks.redis = {
          status: 'unhealthy',
          error: 'Redis connection refused',
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        };
      }
    } else {
      healthCheck.checks.app = {
        status: 'unhealthy',
        error: error.message,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      };
    }
  }

  // Verifica uso de memória
  const memoryUsage = process.memoryUsage();
  const memoryThreshold = 0.9; // 90%
  
  if (memoryUsage.heapUsed / memoryUsage.heapTotal > memoryThreshold) {
    healthCheck.checks.memory.status = 'warning';
    healthCheck.checks.memory.message = 'High memory usage';
  }

  const statusCode = healthCheck.status === 'healthy' ? 200 : 503;
  res.status(statusCode).json(healthCheck);
});

// Health check simples (para load balancers)
router.get('/simple', (req, res) => {
  res.status(200).json({
    status: 'OK',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    service: 'diyapp-v10-core'
  });
});

// Métricas para Prometheus
router.get('/metrics', (req, res) => {
  const memory = process.memoryUsage();
  const uptime = process.uptime();
  
  const metrics = `
# HELP process_cpu_user_seconds_total Total user CPU time spent in seconds.
# TYPE process_cpu_user_seconds_total counter
process_cpu_user_seconds_total ${process.cpuUsage().user / 1000000}

# HELP process_cpu_system_seconds_total Total system CPU time spent in seconds.
# TYPE process_cpu_system_seconds_total counter
process_cpu_system_seconds_total ${process.cpuUsage().system / 1000000}

# HELP process_resident_memory_bytes Resident memory size in bytes.
# TYPE process_resident_memory_bytes gauge
process_resident_memory_bytes ${memory.rss}

# HELP process_heap_bytes Process heap size in bytes.
# TYPE process_heap_bytes gauge
process_heap_bytes ${memory.heapTotal}

# HELP process_heap_used_bytes Process heap used in bytes.
# TYPE process_heap_used_bytes gauge
process_heap_used_bytes ${memory.heapUsed}

# HELP process_uptime_seconds Process uptime in seconds.
# TYPE process_uptime_seconds gauge
process_uptime_seconds ${uptime}

# HELP nodejs_version_info Node.js version info.
# TYPE nodejs_version_info gauge
nodejs_version_info{version="${process.version}"} 1

# HELP app_http_requests_total Total HTTP requests.
# TYPE app_http_requests_total counter
app_http_requests_total{method="get",endpoint="/health"} 1
`;

  res.set('Content-Type', 'text/plain');
  res.send(metrics);
});

module.exports = router;
```

## 6. Scripts de Health Check

`scripts/health-check.sh`:
```bash
#!/bin/bash

# DIYAPP V10 Core - Health Check Script
# SRE Senior - Monitoramento de Confiabilidade

set -e



### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
```typescript
// src/App.tsx - Ponto de entrada principal
import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { ErrorBoundary } from 'react-error-boundary';
import { Toaster } from 'react-hot-toast';

// Design System Tokens
import { ThemeProvider } from './design-system/ThemeProvider';
import { GlobalStyles } from './design-system/GlobalStyles';

// Layout Components
import { MainLayout } from './layouts/MainLayout';
import { AuthLayout } from './layouts/AuthLayout';

// Pages
import { DashboardPage } from './pages/DashboardPage';
import { ProjectListPage } from './pages/ProjectListPage';
import { ProjectDetailPage } from './pages/ProjectDetailPage';
import { TaskBoardPage } from './pages/TaskBoardPage';
import { LoginPage } from './pages/LoginPage';
import { RegisterPage } from './pages/RegisterPage';
import { SettingsPage } from './pages/SettingsPage';
import { NotFoundPage } from './pages/NotFoundPage';

// Store (Zustand)
import { useAuthStore } from './stores/authStore';

// Error Components
import { ErrorFallback } from './components/feedback/ErrorFallback';
import { LoadingScreen } from './components/feedback/LoadingScreen';

// Query Client Configuration
const queryClient = new QueryClient({
  defaultOptions: {
    queries: {
      staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000, // 5 minutes
      retry: 2,
      retryDelay: attemptIndex => Math.min(1000 * 2 ** attemptIndex, 30000),
    },
  },
});

// Protected Route Component
const ProtectedRoute: React.FC<{ children: React.ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
  const { isAuthenticated, isLoading } = useAuthStore();
  
  if (isLoading) {
    return <LoadingScreen />;
  }
  
  if (!isAuthenticated) {
    return <Navigate to="/login" replace />;
  }
  
  return <>{children}</>;
};

// Public Route Component (redirects if authenticated)
const PublicRoute: React.FC<{ children: React.ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
  const { isAuthenticated, isLoading } = useAuthStore();
  
  if (isLoading) {
    return <LoadingScreen />;
  }
  
  if (isAuthenticated) {
    return <Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />;
  }
  
  return <>{children}</>;
};

function App() {
  return (
    <ErrorBoundary FallbackComponent={ErrorFallback}>
      <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
        <ThemeProvider>
          <GlobalStyles />
          <Router>
            <Routes>
              {/* Public Routes */}
              <Route path="/login" element={
                <PublicRoute>
                  <AuthLayout>
                    <LoginPage />
                  </AuthLayout>
                </PublicRoute>
              } />
              
              <Route path="/register" element={
                <PublicRoute>
                  <AuthLayout>
                    <RegisterPage />
                  </AuthLayout>
                </PublicRoute>
              } />
              
              {/* Protected Routes */}
              <Route path="/" element={
                <ProtectedRoute>
                  <MainLayout />
                </ProtectedRoute>
              }>
                <Route index element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
                <Route path="dashboard" element={<DashboardPage />} />
                <Route path="projects" element={<ProjectListPage />} />
                <Route path="projects/:projectId" element={<ProjectDetailPage />} />
                <Route path="tasks" element={<TaskBoardPage />} />
                <Route path="settings" element={<SettingsPage />} />
              </Route>
              
              {/* 404 */}
              <Route path="*" element={<NotFoundPage />} />
            </Routes>
          </Router>
          <Toaster 
            position="top-right"
            toastOptions={{
              duration: 4000,
              style: {
                background: 'var(--color-surface)',
                color: 'var(--color-text-primary)',
                border: '1px solid var(--color-border)',
              },
            }}
          />
        </ThemeProvider>
      </QueryClientProvider>
    </ErrorBoundary>
  );
}

export default App;
```

    banner: 1200,
    overlay: 1300,
    modal: 1400,
    popover: 1500,
    toast: 1700,
    tooltip: 1800,
  },
} as const;

// Theme Context
type Theme = 'light' | 'dark';

interface ThemeContextType {
  theme: Theme;
  toggleTheme: () => void;
  setTheme: (theme: Theme) => void;
}

const ThemeContext = createContext<ThemeContextType | undefined>(undefined);

export const useTheme = () => {
  const context = useContext(ThemeContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('useTheme must be used within a ThemeProvider');
  }
  return context;
};

interface ThemeProviderProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

export const ThemeProvider: React.FC<ThemeProviderProps> = ({ children }) => {
  const [theme, setTheme] = useState<Theme>(() => {
    const savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('theme') as Theme;
    return savedTheme || 'light';
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    const root = document.documentElement;
    
    if (theme === 'dark') {
      root.classList.add('dark');
    } else {
      root.classList.remove('dark');
    }
    
    localStorage.setItem('theme', theme);
  }, [theme]);

  const toggleTheme = () => {
    setTheme(prev => prev === 'light' ? 'dark' : 'light');
  };

  const value = {
    theme,
    toggleTheme,
    setTheme,
  };

  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value={value}>
      {children}
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
};
```

```typescript
// src/design-system/GlobalStyles.tsx
import { createGlobalStyle } from 'styled-components';
import { tokens } from './ThemeProvider';

export const GlobalStyles = createGlobalStyle`
  :root {

# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Sistema de Testes Automatizados

## Estrutura do Projeto de Testes

```
tests/
├── e2e/
│   ├── cypress/
│   │   ├── fixtures/
│   │   ├── integration/
│   │   │   ├── auth/
│   │   │   ├── chat/
│   │   │   ├── agents/
│   │   │   └── dashboard/
│   │   ├── plugins/
│   │   ├── support/

│   └── playwright/
│       ├── tests/
│       ├── fixtures/
│       └── playwright.config.js
├── integration/

## 1. Configuração Principal (package.json)

```json
{
  "name": "diyapp-v10-tests",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "scripts": {
    "test:unit": "jest --config jest.config.js",
    "test:integration": "jest --config jest.integration.config.js",
    "test:e2e:cypress": "cypress run",
    "test:e2e:cypress:open": "cypress open",
    "test:e2e:playwright": "playwright test",
    "test:llm": "node tests/llm/runner.js",
    "test:smoke": "cypress run --config-file=cypress.smoke.json",
    "test:regression": "cypress run --config-file=cypress.regression.json",
    "test:ci": "npm run test:unit && npm run test:integration && npm run test:smoke",
    "test:full": "npm run test:unit && npm run test:integration && npm run test:e2e:cypress && npm run test:llm",
    "lint:tests": "eslint tests/ --ext .js,.ts",
    "generate:coverage": "nyc report --reporter=html",
    "test:flaky:detect": "node scripts/detect-flaky-tests.js"
  },

## 4. Suporte Cypress (e2e/cypress/support/index.js)

```javascript
// Import commands.js
import './commands';
import '@testing-library/cypress/add-commands';

// Global beforeEach hook
beforeEach(() => {
  // Clear cookies and localStorage
  cy.clearCookies();
  cy.clearLocalStorage();
  
  // Log test start
  const testName = Cypress.currentTest.title;
  const suiteName = Cypress.currentTest.titlePath[0];
  cy.log(`Starting test: ${suiteName} - ${testName}`);
});

// Global afterEach hook
afterEach(function() {
  if (this.currentTest.state === 'failed') {
    // Take screenshot on failure
    const screenshotFileName = `${Cypress.spec.name} -- ${this.currentTest.title} (failed)`;
    cy.screenshot(screenshotFileName, { overwrite: true });
    
    // Log failure details
    cy.task('logTestFailure', {
      spec: Cypress.spec.name,
      test: this.currentTest.title,
      state: this.currentTest.state,
      error: this.currentTest.err?.message
    });
  }
});

// Custom commands
Cypress.Commands.add('login', (email, password) => {
  cy.session([email, password], () => {
    cy.visit('/login');
    cy.get('[data-testid="email-input"]').type(email);
    cy.get('[data-testid="password-input"]').type(password);
    cy.get('[data-testid="login-button"]').click();
    cy.url().should('include', '/dashboard');
    cy.get('[data-testid="user-avatar"]').should('be.visible');
  });
});

Cypress.Commands.add('createAgent', (agentData) => {
  cy.get('[data-testid="create-agent-button"]').click();
  cy.get('[data-testid="agent-name-input"]').type(agentData.name);
  cy.get('[data-testid="agent-description-input"]').type(agentData.description);
  
  if (agentData.instructions) {
    cy.get('[data-testid="agent-instructions-textarea"]').type(agentData.instructions);
  }
  
  cy.get('[data-testid="save-agent-button"]').click();
  cy.get('[data-testid="agent-created-success"]').should('be.visible');
});

Cypress.Commands.add('sendChatMessage', (message) => {
  cy.get('[data-testid="chat-input"]').type(message);
  cy.get('[data-testid="send-message-button"]').click();
  cy.get('[data-testid="message-loading"]').should('be.visible');
  cy.get('[data-testid="message-loading"]', { timeout: 30000 }).should('not.exist');
  cy.get('[data-testid="chat-message"]').last().should('contain.text', message);
});
```

## 5. Testes E2E Baseados em Critérios Gherkin

### 5.1 Autenticação (e2e/cypress/integration/auth/auth.spec.js)

```javascript
/// <reference types="cypress" />

describe('Autenticação do Usuário', () => {
  beforeEach(() => {
    cy.visit('/');
  });

  describe('Cenário: Login bem-sucedido', () => {
    it('Dado que estou na página de login', () => {
      cy.visit('/login');
      cy.url().should('include', '/login');
      cy.get('[data-testid="login-form"]').should('be.visible');
    });

    it('Quando insiro credenciais válidas', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="email-input"]').type(Cypress.env('TEST_USER_EMAIL'));
      cy.get('[data-testid="password-input"]').type(Cypress.env('TEST_USER_PASSWORD'));
    });

    it('E clico no botão de login', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="login-button"]').click();
    });

    it('Então devo ser redirecionado para o dashboard', () => {
      cy.url().should('include', '/dashboard');
    });

    it('E devo ver meu nome de usuário exibido', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="user-greeting"]').should('contain.text', 'Bem-vindo');
    });
  });

  describe('Cenário: Login com credenciais inválidas', () => {
    it('Dado que estou na página de login', () => {
      cy.visit('/login');
    });

    it('Quando insiro um email inválido', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="email-input"]').type('email-invalido@teste.com');
      cy.get('[data-testid="password-input"]').type('senha123');
    });

    it('E clico no botão de login', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="login-button"]').click();
    });

    it('Então devo ver uma mensagem de erro', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="error-message"]')
        .should('be.visible')
        .and('contain.text', 'Credenciais inválidas');
    });

    it('E não devo ser redirecionado para o dashboard', () => {
      cy.url().should('include', '/login');
    });
  });

  describe('Cenário: Logout do sistema', () => {
    beforeEach(() => {
      cy.login(Cypress.env('TEST_USER_EMAIL'), Cypress.env('TEST_USER_PASSWORD'));
    });

    it('Dado que estou logado no sistema', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="user-avatar"]').should('be.visible');
    });

    it('Quando clico no menu do usuário', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="user-menu"]').click();
    });

    it('E seleciono a opção "Sair"', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="logout-button"]').click();
    });

    it('Então devo ser redirecionado para a página de login', () => {
      cy.url().should('include', '/login');
    });

    it('E não devo conseguir acessar páginas protegidas', () => {
      cy.visit('/dashboard');
      cy.url().should('include', '/login');
    });
  });
});
```

### 5.2 Chat com Agentes (e2e/cypress/integration/chat/chat.spec.js)

```javascript
/// <reference types="cypress" />

describe('Sistema de Chat com Agentes', () => {
  beforeEach(() => {
    cy.login(Cypress.env('TEST_USER_EMAIL'), Cypress.env('TEST_USER_PASSWORD'));
    cy.visit('/chat');
  });

  describe('Cenário: Enviar mensagem para agente', () => {
    it('Dado que estou na página de chat', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="chat-container"]').should('be.visible');
    });

    it('E tenho um agente selecionado', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="agent-selector"]').select('Assistant');
      cy.get('[data-testid="selected-agent-name"]').should('contain.text', 'Assistant');
    });

    it('Quando digito uma mensagem no campo de entrada', () => {
      const testMessage = 'Qual é a capital da França?';
      cy.get('[data-testid="chat-input"]').type(testMessage);
    });

    it('E clico no botão enviar', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="send-message-button"]').click();
    });

    it('Então devo ver minha mensagem na conversa', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="user-message"]').last().should('contain.text', 'capital da França');
    });

    it('E devo ver uma resposta do agente', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="agent-response"]', { timeout: 30000 })
        .last()
        .should('be.visible')
        .and('contain.text', 'Paris');
    });

    it('E o campo de entrada deve ser limpo', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="chat-input"]').should('have.value', '');
    });
  });

  describe('Cenário: Trocar de agente durante conversa', () => {
    it('Dado que estou conversando com o agente "Assistant"', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="agent-selector"]').select('Assistant');
      cy.sendChatMessage('Olá, Assistant!');
    });

    it('Quando seleciono o agente "Code Helper"', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="agent-selector"]').select('Code Helper');
    });

    it('Então o histórico de conversa deve ser limpo', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="chat-message"]').should('not.exist');
    });

    it('E o novo agente deve estar selecionado', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="selected-agent-name"]').should('contain.text', 'Code Helper');
    });
  });

  describe('Cenário: Enviar mensagem vazia', () => {
    it('Dado que estou na página de chat', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="chat-container"]').should('be.visible');
    });

    it('Quando clico no botão enviar sem digitar mensagem', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="send-message-button"]').click();
    });

    it('Então nenhuma mensagem deve ser enviada', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="user-message"]').should('not.exist');
    });

    it('E devo ver uma validação no campo de entrada', () => {
      cy.get('[data-testid="chat-input"]').should('have.attr', 'aria-invalid', 'true');
    });
  });
});
```

      cy.get('[data-testid="success-message"]').should('be.visible');
    });
  });

  describe('Cenário: Excluir agente', () => {
    it('Dado que tenho um agente na lista', () => {
      cy.get('[data

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Esquema de Banco de Dados

## 1. Análise do Contexto e Requisitos

Para a V10, precisamos modelar um esquema que suporte:
1. **Recursos de IA** (LLM Gateway, custos, avaliações)
2. **Métricas de produto** (eventos, funis, adoção)
3. **Dados operacionais** (deploys, incidentes, custos)
4. **Conformidade** (retenção, anonimização, auditoria)

## 2. Estrutura de Diretórios

```
diyapp-v10-database/
├── src/
│   ├── models/
│   │   ├── v9_legacy/
│   │   ├── v10_core/
│   │   └── migrations/
│   ├── scripts/
│   │   ├── migration/
│   │   └── optimization/
│   └── tests/
├── dbt/
│   ├── models/
│   │   ├── staging/
│   │   ├── marts/
│   │   └── tests/
│   └── dbt_project.yml
├── sql/
│   ├── optimization/
│   └── migration/
├── docs/
│   └── data_dictionary.md
└── index.html
```

## 3. Esquema V10 Core (PostgreSQL)

### 3.1. Schema Principal

```sql
-- src/models/v10_core/schema_v10.sql
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS v10_core;
SET search_path TO v10_core;

-- ==================== TABELAS DE PRODUTO ====================
CREATE TABLE users (
    user_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    external_id VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(255),
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    metadata JSONB,
    -- GDPR compliance
    data_retention_until TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    anonymized_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    region VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'global'
);

CREATE TABLE events (
    event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(user_id),
    session_id VARCHAR(255),
    event_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    event_type VARCHAR(50) CHECK (event_type IN ('page_view', 'click', 'api_call', 'llm_interaction', 'error')),
    properties JSONB,
    device_info JSONB,
    ip_address INET,
    user_agent TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    -- Partitioning key
    event_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (created_at::DATE) STORED
) PARTITION BY RANGE (event_date);

-- Partições mensais para events
CREATE TABLE events_2024_01 PARTITION OF events
    FOR VALUES FROM ('2024-01-01') TO ('2024-02-01');

CREATE TABLE events_2024_02 PARTITION OF events
    FOR VALUES FROM ('2024-02-01') TO ('2024-03-01');

-- ==================== TABELAS DE IA/LLM ====================
CREATE TABLE llm_providers (
    provider_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    api_base_url VARCHAR(255),
    cost_per_1k_input_tokens DECIMAL(10,6),
    cost_per_1k_output_tokens DECIMAL(10,6),
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE llm_models (
    model_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    provider_id INTEGER REFERENCES llm_providers(provider_id),
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    context_length INTEGER,
    max_output_tokens INTEGER,
    is_fine_tunable BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(provider_id, model_name)
);

CREATE TABLE llm_calls (
    call_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(user_id),
    session_id VARCHAR(255),
    model_id INTEGER REFERENCES llm_models(model_id),
    provider_id INTEGER REFERENCES llm_providers(provider_id),
    
    -- Input/Output metrics
    input_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    output_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    total_tokens INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_tokens + output_tokens) STORED,
    
    -- Cost calculation
    input_cost DECIMAL(12,6) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        input_tokens::DECIMAL / 1000 * (
            SELECT cost_per_1k_input_tokens 
            FROM llm_providers p 
            WHERE p.provider_id = llm_calls.provider_id
        )
    ) STORED,
    
    output_cost DECIMAL(12,6) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        output_tokens::DECIMAL / 1000 * (
            SELECT cost_per_1k_output_tokens 
            FROM llm_providers p 
            WHERE p.provider_id = llm_calls.provider_id
        )
    ) STORED,
    
    total_cost DECIMAL(12,6) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (input_cost + output_cost) STORED,
    
    -- Performance metrics
    latency_ms INTEGER,
    success BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    error_message TEXT,
    
    -- Request/Response (anonymized for compliance)
    prompt_hash VARCHAR(64), -- SHA256 of anonymized prompt
    response_hash VARCHAR(64), -- SHA256 of response
    
    -- Feature tracking
    feature_name VARCHAR(100),
    sub_feature VARCHAR(100),
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    call_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (created_at::DATE) STORED
) PARTITION BY RANGE (call_date);

-- ==================== TABELAS OPERACIONAIS ====================
CREATE TABLE deployments (
    deployment_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    service_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    version VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    environment VARCHAR(50) CHECK (environment IN ('development', 'staging', 'production')),
    deployed_by VARCHAR(255),
    status VARCHAR(50) CHECK (status IN ('success', 'failure', 'rollback')),
    duration_seconds INTEGER,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    metadata JSONB
);

CREATE TABLE incidents (
    incident_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    severity VARCHAR(20) CHECK (severity IN ('critical', 'high', 'medium', 'low')),
    service_name VARCHAR(100),
    status VARCHAR(50) CHECK (status IN ('open', 'investigating', 'resolved', 'closed')),
    opened_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    resolved_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    mttr_seconds INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (resolved_at - opened_at))
    ) STORED,
    root_cause TEXT,
    resolution TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- ==================== TABELAS DE FINE-TUNING ====================
CREATE TABLE fine_tuning_datasets (
    dataset_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    model_id INTEGER REFERENCES llm_models(model_id),
    
    -- Dataset metrics
    total_examples INTEGER,
    total_tokens INTEGER,
    
    -- Compliance tracking
    anonymization_method VARCHAR(100),
    anonymized_by VARCHAR(255),
    anonymized_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Quality metrics
    quality_score DECIMAL(3,2),
    validation_split_percent INTEGER DEFAULT 20,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'active'
);

CREATE TABLE fine_tuning_jobs (
    job_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    dataset_id UUID REFERENCES fine_tuning_datasets(dataset_id),
    base_model_id INTEGER REFERENCES llm_models(model_id),
    fine_tuned_model_name VARCHAR(255),
    
    -- Training metrics
    training_loss DECIMAL(10,6),
    validation_loss DECIMAL(10,6),
    epochs INTEGER,
    batch_size INTEGER,
    
    -- Cost tracking
    training_tokens INTEGER,
    training_cost DECIMAL(12,6),
    
    -- Status
    status VARCHAR(50) CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'running', 'completed', 'failed')),
    started_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    completed_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- ==================== TABELAS DE CONFORMIDADE ====================
CREATE TABLE data_retention_policies (
    policy_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    table_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    retention_days INTEGER NOT NULL,
    anonymize_before_delete BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_by VARCHAR(255)
);

CREATE TABLE data_access_audit (
    audit_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    user_id VARCHAR(255),
    action VARCHAR(50) CHECK (action IN ('select', 'insert', 'update', 'delete', 'export')),
    table_name VARCHAR(255),
    record_count INTEGER,
    query_hash VARCHAR(64),
    ip_address INET,
    user_agent TEXT,
    accessed_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- ==================== ÍNDICES ====================
-- Users
CREATE INDEX idx_users_email ON users(email);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_created_at ON users(created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_region ON users(region);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_retention ON users(data_retention_until) WHERE data_retention_until IS NOT NULL;

-- Events
CREATE INDEX idx_events_user_date ON events(user_id, event_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_events_name_date ON events(event_name, event_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_events_session ON events(session_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_events_type ON events(event_type);

-- LLM Calls
CREATE INDEX idx_llm_calls_user_date ON llm_calls(user_id, call_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_llm_calls_model_date ON llm_calls(model_id, call_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_llm_calls_feature_date ON llm_calls(feature_name, call_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_llm_calls_cost_date ON llm_calls(total_cost, call_date);

-- Fine-tuning
CREATE INDEX idx_ft_datasets_model ON fine_tuning_datasets(model_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_ft_jobs_status ON fine_tuning_jobs(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_ft_jobs_dataset ON fine_tuning_jobs(dataset_id);

-- Audit
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_user_time ON data_access_audit(user_id, accessed_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_action ON data_access_audit(action, accessed_at);
```

## 4. Scripts de Migração V9 → V10

```sql
-- src/scripts/migration/v9_to_v10_migration.sql
-- Migration script with data validation and rollback capability

BEGIN;

-- Create migration tracking table if not exists
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS v10_core.migration_log (
    migration_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    migration_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR(50) CHECK (status IN ('started', 'completed', 'failed', 'rolled_back')),
    rows_affected INTEGER,
    started_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    completed_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    error_message TEXT
);

-- Start migration tracking
INSERT INTO v10_core.migration_log (migration_name, status, started_at)
VALUES ('v9_to_v10_core_migration', 'started', CURRENT_TIMESTAMP);

-- 1. Migrate users from legacy schema
DO $$
DECLARE
    migrated_users INTEGER;
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO v10_core.users (
        external_id, 
        email, 
        name, 
        created_at, 
        updated_at, 
        is_active,
        metadata,
        region
    )
    SELECT 
        u.id::VARCHAR,
        COALESCE(u.email, 'anonymous_' || u.id || '@diyapp.com'),
        COALESCE(u.full_name, 'User ' || u.id),
        COALESCE(u.created_at, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP - INTERVAL '1 year'),
        COALESCE(u.updated_at, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP),
        COALESCE(u.is_active, TRUE),
        jsonb_build_object(
            'legacy_id', u.id,
            'source', 'v9_migration'
        ),
        COALESCE(u.region, 'global')
    FROM legacy.users u
    WHERE u.deleted_at IS NULL
    ON CONFLICT (email) DO UPDATE SET
        name = EXCLUDED.name,
        updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
        metadata = v10_core.users.metadata || EXCLUDED.metadata;
    
    GET DIAGNOSTICS migrated_users = ROW_COUNT;
    
    -- Log migration
    UPDATE v10_core.migration_log 
    SET rows_affected = migrated_users
    WHERE migration_name = 'v9_to_v10_core_migration'
    AND status = 'started';
    
    RAISE NOTICE 'Migrated % users from V9', migrated_users;
END $$;

-- 2. Migrate events with data quality checks
DO $$
DECLARE
    migrated_events INTEGER;
    invalid_events INTEGER;
BEGIN
    -- First, identify invalid events
    CREATE TEMP TABLE invalid_legacy_events AS
    SELECT e.id
    FROM legacy.events e
    LEFT JOIN v10_core.users u ON e.user_id::VARCHAR = u.external_id
    WHERE e.user_id IS NOT NULL AND u.user_id IS NULL;
    
    GET DIAGNOSTICS invalid_events = ROW_COUNT;
    
    -- Migrate valid events
    INSERT INTO v10_core.events (
        user_id,
        session_id,
        event_name,
        event_type,
        properties,
        device_info,
        ip_address,
        user_agent,
        created_at
    )
    SELECT 
        u.user_id,
        e.session_id,
        COALESCE(e.event_name, 'unknown_event'),
        CASE 
            WHEN e.event_type IN ('page_view', 'click', 'api_call') THEN e.event_type
            ELSE 'api_call'
        END,
        COALESCE(e.properties::jsonb, '{}'::jsonb),
        COALESCE(e.device_info::jsonb, '{}'::jsonb),
        e.ip_address::inet,
        e.user_agent,
        COALESCE(e.created_at, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)
    FROM legacy.events e
    LEFT JOIN v10_core.users u ON e.user_id::VARCHAR = u.external_id
    WHERE e.id NOT IN (SELECT id FROM invalid_legacy_events)
    AND e.created_at >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '90 days' -- Only migrate last 90 days
    ORDER BY e.created_at;
    
    GET DIAGNOSTICS migrated_events = ROW_COUNT;
    
    -- Log invalid events for manual review
    INSERT INTO v10_core.migration_log (migration_name, status, rows_affected, error_message)
    VALUES ('v9_events_validation', 'failed', invalid_events, 
            FORMAT('%s events with invalid user references found', invalid_events));
    
    RAISE NOTICE 'Migrated % events, % invalid events skipped', migrated_events, invalid_events;
    
    DROP TABLE invalid_legacy_events;
END $$;

-- 3. Create default LLM providers
INSERT INTO v10_core.llm_providers (name, api_base_url, cost_per_1k_input_tokens, cost_per_1k_output_tokens)
VALUES 
    ('openai', 'https://api.openai.com/v1', 0.0015, 0.002),
    ('anthropic', 'https://api.anthropic.com/v1', 0.003, 0.015),
    ('google', 'https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1', 0.0005, 0.0015),
    ('azure', 'https://{resource}.openai.azure.com', 0.001, 0.002)
ON CONFLICT (name) DO NOTHING;

-- 4. Create default LLM models
INSERT INTO v10_core.llm_models (provider_id, model_name, context_length, max_output_tokens, is_fine_tunable)
SELECT 
    p.provider_id,
    m.model_name,
    m.context_length,
    m.max_output_tokens,
    m.is_fine_tunable
FROM (VALUES
    ('gpt-4-turbo-preview', 128000, 4096, true),
    ('gpt-3.5-turbo', 16385, 4096, true),
    ('claude-3-opus', 200000, 4096, false),
    ('gemini-pro', 32768, 8192, false)
) AS m(model_name, context_length, max_output_tokens, is_fine_tunable)
CROSS JOIN v10_core.llm_providers p
WHERE p.name IN ('openai', 'anthropic', 'google')
ON CONFLICT (provider_id, model_name) DO UPDATE SET
    context_length = EXCLUDED.context_length,
    max_output_tokens = EXCLUDED.max_output_tokens;

-- 5. Set up data retention policies
INSERT INTO v10_core.data_retention_policies (table_name, retention_days, anonymize_before_delete, created_by)
VALUES
    ('events', 365, true, 'system'),
    ('llm_calls', 180, true, 'system'),
    ('users', 730, false, 'system'),
    ('data_access_audit', 1095, false, 'system')
ON CONFLICT (table_name) DO UPDATE SET
    retention_days = EXCLUDED.retention_days,
   

### [Sessão Paralela: Inovação]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Integração com API de IA Generativa

## Análise de Oportunidade (H2 - Expandir o produto)

**Sinal identificado**: Usuários do DIYAPP frequentemente solicitam sugestões automáticas para projetos baseados em materiais disponíveis e nível de habilidade.

**Hipótese**: Acreditamos que usuários iniciantes em projetos DIY têm dificuldade em gerar ideias criativas com materiais limitados e que a integração com uma API de IA generativa para sugestões personalizadas vai aumentar em 25% a taxa de conclusão de projetos em 30 dias.

**Experimento proposto**: Implementar um módulo de sugestões automáticas usando a API gratuita do Hugging Face (Inference API) para gerar ideias de projetos baseadas em materiais de entrada do usuário.

## Arquitetura da Solução

```
DIYAPP Evolution V10/
├── src/
│   ├── ai-suggestions/
│   │   ├── huggingface-client.js
│   │   ├── suggestion-engine.js
│   │   └── prompt-templates.js
│   ├── controllers/
│   │   └── ai-suggestions-controller.js
│   ├── middleware/
│   │   └── rate-limiter.js
│   └── utils/
│       └── logger.js
├── public/
│   ├── index.html (Dashboard principal)
│   ├── css/
│   │   └── ai-suggestions.css
│   └── js/
│       └── ai-suggestions-ui.js
├── config/
│   └── ai-config.js
├── tests/
│   └── ai-suggestions.test.js
├── package.json
└── README.md
```

## Implementação Completa

### 2. Configuração da API de IA (config/ai-config.js)
```javascript
// Configurações para APIs de IA generativa
// Usando Hugging Face Inference API (gratuita para testes)

const AI_CONFIG = {
  // Hugging Face Inference API (modelo gratuito para texto)
  HUGGING_FACE: {
    API_URL: 'https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models',
    MODELS: {
      TEXT_GENERATION: 'gpt2', // Modelo gratuito para testes
      // Alternativas premium quando escalar:
      // 'microsoft/DialoGPT-medium',
      // 'google/flan-t5-base'
    },
    API_KEY: process.env.HUGGING_FACE_API_KEY || 'demo_key_for_testing',
    RATE_LIMIT: {
      FREE: 10000, // requests por mês no plano gratuito
      PER_MINUTE: 10 // requests por minuto
    }
  },
  
  // Fallback para quando a API estiver indisponível
  FALLBACK_SUGGESTIONS: [
    "Crie uma estante de livros com caixotes de madeira",
    "Transforme garrafas de vidro em vasos decorativos",
    "Faça um organizador de ferramentas com tubos de PVC",
    "Construa uma mesa de centro com pallets reciclados",
    "Crie luminárias com latas de alumínio decoradas"
  ],
  
  // Categorias de projetos DIY
  PROJECT_CATEGORIES: [
    'Madeira',
    'Metal',
    'Tecido',
    'Papelão',
    'Reciclados',
    'Eletrônicos',
    'Jardim',
    'Decoração'
  ],
  
  // Níveis de dificuldade
  DIFFICULTY_LEVELS: [
    { id: 'beginner', name: 'Iniciante', time: '2-4 horas' },
    { id: 'intermediate', name: 'Intermediário', time: '1-2 dias' },
    { id: 'advanced', name: 'Avançado', time: '3+ dias' }
  ]
};

module.exports = AI_CONFIG;
```

### 3. Cliente Hugging Face (src/ai-suggestions/huggingface-client.js)
```javascript
const axios = require('axios');
const AI_CONFIG = require('../../config/ai-config');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

class HuggingFaceClient {
  constructor() {
    this.apiKey = AI_CONFIG.HUGGING_FACE.API_KEY;
    this.baseURL = AI_CONFIG.HUGGING_FACE.API_URL;
    this.model = AI_CONFIG.HUGGING_FACE.MODELS.TEXT_GENERATION;
    
    this.client = axios.create({
      baseURL: this.baseURL,
      headers: {
        'Authorization': `Bearer ${this.apiKey}`,
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
      },
      timeout: 30000 // 30 segundos timeout
    });
    
    this.isAvailable = true;
    this.testConnection();
  }
  
  async testConnection() {
    try {
      // Teste simples de conexão
      const response = await this.client.get(`/${this.model}`, {
        timeout: 5000
      });
      
      if (response.status === 200) {
        logger.info('Hugging Face API conectada com sucesso');
        this.isAvailable = true;
      }
    } catch (error) {
      logger.warn(`Hugging Face API indisponível: ${error.message}`);
      this.isAvailable = false;
    }
  }
  
  async generateText(prompt, maxLength = 150) {
    if (!this.isAvailable) {
      throw new Error('API de IA temporariamente indisponível');
    }
    
    try {
      const response = await this.client.post(
        `/${this.model}`,
        {
          inputs: prompt,
          parameters: {
            max_length: maxLength,
            temperature: 0.8,
            top_p: 0.9,
            do_sample: true,
            return_full_text: false
          }
        }
      );
      
      if (response.data && response.data[0] && response.data[0].generated_text) {
        return response.data[0].generated_text.trim();
      }
      
      throw new Error('Resposta da API em formato inesperado');
      
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Erro na geração de texto: ${error.message}`);
      
      // Fallback para desenvolvimento/testes
      if (error.response && error.response.status === 503) {
        // Modelo carregando - usar fallback
        return this.getFallbackSuggestion();
      }
      
      throw error;
    }
  }
  
  getFallbackSuggestion() {
    const suggestions = AI_CONFIG.FALLBACK_SUGGESTIONS;
    return suggestions[Math.floor(Math.random() * suggestions.length)];
  }
  
  async getModelStatus() {
    try {
      const response = await this.client.get(`/${this.model}`);
      return {
        available: true,
        model: response.data.modelId,
        status: 'online'
      };
    } catch (error) {
      return {
        available: false,
        error: error.message,
        status: 'offline'
      };
    }
  }
}

module.exports = new HuggingFaceClient();
```

### 4. Engine de Sugestões (src/ai-suggestions/suggestion-engine.js)
```javascript
const huggingFaceClient = require('./huggingface-client');
const AI_CONFIG = require('../../config/ai-config');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');
const promptTemplates = require('./prompt-templates');

class SuggestionEngine {
  constructor() {
    this.cache = new Map();
    this.cacheDuration = 3600000; // 1 hora em milissegundos
  }
  
  async generateProjectSuggestions(userInput) {
    const {
      materials = [],
      skillLevel = 'beginner',
      category = 'Geral',
      availableTime = '4 horas',
      budget = 'baixo'
    } = userInput;
    
    // Verificar cache primeiro
    const cacheKey = this.generateCacheKey(materials, skillLevel, category);
    const cached = this.cache.get(cacheKey);
    
    if (cached && (Date.now() - cached.timestamp) < this.cacheDuration) {
      logger.info(`Retornando sugestão do cache: ${cacheKey}`);
      return cached.suggestions;
    }
    
    try {
      // Gerar prompt baseado no template
      const prompt = promptTemplates.generateProjectPrompt({
        materials,
        skillLevel,
        category,
        availableTime,
        budget
      });
      
      // Chamar API de IA
      const aiResponse = await huggingFaceClient.generateText(prompt, 200);
      
      // Processar resposta
      const suggestions = this.parseAIResponse(aiResponse);
      
      // Validar sugestões
      const validatedSuggestions = this.validateSuggestions(suggestions, materials);
      
      // Adicionar metadados
      const enhancedSuggestions = validatedSuggestions.map(suggestion => ({
        ...suggestion,
        id: this.generateId(),
        materials: this.extractMaterials(suggestion.description),
        estimatedTime: this.estimateTime(suggestion.description, skillLevel),
        difficulty: skillLevel,
        category: category,
        generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        source: 'ai'
      }));
      
      // Armazenar em cache
      this.cache.set(cacheKey, {
        timestamp: Date.now(),
        suggestions: enhancedSuggestions
      });
      
      logger.info(`Geradas ${enhancedSuggestions.length} sugestões para: ${materials.join(', ')}`);
      
      return enhancedSuggestions;
      
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Erro ao gerar sugestões: ${error.message}`);
      
      // Fallback para sugestões pré-definidas
      return this.getFallbackSuggestions(materials, skillLevel, category);
    }
  }
  
  generateCacheKey(materials, skillLevel, category) {
    return `${materials.sort().join('-')}-${skillLevel}-${category}`.toLowerCase();
  }
  
  parseAIResponse(response) {
    // Tentar extrair múltiplas sugestões da resposta da IA
    const lines = response.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim().length > 0);
    
    return lines.slice(0, 5).map((line, index) => ({
      title: this.extractTitle(line),
      description: line.trim(),
      steps: this.extractSteps(line)
    }));
  }
  
  extractTitle(text) {
    // Extrair um título da primeira frase
    const firstSentence = text.split('.')[0];
    return firstSentence.length > 60 
      ? firstSentence.substring(0, 60) + '...' 
      : firstSentence;
  }
  
  extractSteps(text) {
    // Extrair passos numerados ou com marcadores
    const steps = [];
    const stepRegex = /(\d+\.\s|[•\-]\s)(.+?)(?=\n\d+\.|\n[•\-]|$)/g;
    let match;
    
    while ((match = stepRegex.exec(text)) !== null) {
      steps.push(match[2].trim());
    }
    
    return steps.length > 0 ? steps : [
      'Prepare os materiais',
      'Siga as instruções básicas',
      'Finalize e teste o projeto'
    ];
  }
  
  validateSuggestions(suggestions, availableMaterials) {
    return suggestions.filter(suggestion => {
      const suggestionMaterials = this.extractMaterials(suggestion.description);
      
      // Verificar se pelo menos 60% dos materiais sugeridos estão disponíveis
      const availableCount = suggestionMaterials.filter(material => 
        availableMaterials.some(available => 
          available.toLowerCase().includes(material.toLowerCase()) ||
          material.toLowerCase().includes(available.toLowerCase())
        )
      ).length;
      
      return availableCount >= Math.max(1, suggestionMaterials.length * 0.6);
    });
  }
  
  extractMaterials(description) {
    // Lista comum de materiais DIY
    const commonMaterials = [
      'madeira', 'parafuso', 'pregos', 'cola', 'tinta', 'pincel',
      'tecido', 'linha', 'agulha', 'papel', 'cartolina', 'tesoura',
      'plástico', 'metal', 'fio', 'lâmpada', 'bateria', 'ferramenta',
      'martelo', 'serra', 'furadeira', 'lixa', 'verniz'
    ];
    
    return commonMaterials.filter(material => 
      description.toLowerCase().includes(material)
    );
  }
  
  estimateTime(description, skillLevel) {
    const wordCount = description.split(' ').length;
    let baseTime = wordCount * 0.5; // minutos base
    
    // Ajustar baseado no nível de habilidade
    if (skillLevel === 'beginner') baseTime *= 1.5;
    if (skillLevel === 'advanced') baseTime *= 0.7;
    
    // Converter para formato legível
    if (baseTime < 60) return `${Math.ceil(baseTime)} minutos`;
    if (baseTime < 300) return `${Math.ceil(baseTime / 60)} horas`;
    return `${Math.ceil(baseTime / 60 / 8)} dias`;
  }
  
  generateId() {
    return `suggestion_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;
  }
  
  getFallbackSuggestions(materials, skillLevel, category) {
    const filtered = AI_CONFIG.FALLBACK_SUGGESTIONS.filter(suggestion => {
      const suggestionLower = suggestion.toLowerCase();
      return materials.some(material => 
        suggestionLower.includes(material.toLowerCase())
      );
    });
    
    return filtered.slice(0, 3).map((suggestion, index) => ({
      id: `fallback_${index}_${Date.now()}`,
      title: suggestion.split(':')[0] || suggestion.substring(0, 50),
      description: suggestion,
      materials: this.extractMaterials(suggestion),
      estimatedTime: '2-4 horas',
      difficulty: skillLevel,
      category: category,
      steps: ['Preparar materiais', 'Seguir instruções básicas', 'Finalizar projeto'],
      generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      source: 'fallback'
    }));
  }
  
  async getEngineStatus() {
    const modelStatus = await huggingFaceClient.getModelStatus();
    
    return {
      aiAvailable: huggingFaceClient.isAvailable,
      modelStatus: modelStatus,
      cacheSize: this.cache.size,
      cacheHits: Array.from(this.cache.values()).filter(
        item => (Date.now() - item.timestamp) < this.cacheDuration
      ).length
    };
  }
}

module.exports = new SuggestionEngine();
```
