### 2.2 Middleware de Rate Limiting

**src/security/middleware/rate-limiter.js:**
```javascript
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const RedisStore = require('rate-limit-redis');
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const { createHash } = require('crypto');

class SecurityRateLimiter {
  constructor() {
    this.redisClient = new Redis({
      host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: process.env.REDIS_PORT || 6379,
      password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD,
      enableOfflineQueue: false,
      retryStrategy: (times) => Math.min(times * 50, 2000)
    });

    this.rateLimiters = this.createLimiters();
  }

  createLimiters() {
    return {
      // Limiter global para APIs públicas
      api: rateLimit({
        store: new RedisStore({
          client: this.redisClient,
          prefix: 'rl:api:'
        }),
        windowMs: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS) || 15 * 60 * 1000,
        max: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS) || 100,
        message: {
          error: 'Too many requests',
          retryAfter: '15 minutes'
        },
        standardHeaders: true,
        legacyHeaders: false,
        keyGenerator: (req) => {
          // Combina IP com user agent para melhor identificação
          const ip = req.ip;
          const ua = req.get('user-agent') || 'unknown';
          const key = `${ip}:${createHash('sha256').update(ua).digest('hex').substring(0, 16)}`;
          return key;
        },
        skip: (req) => {
          // Pular rate limiting para IPs confiáveis (ex: health checks)
          const trustedIPs = ['127.0.0.1', '::1'];
          return trustedIPs.includes(req.ip);
        }
      }),

      // Limiter mais restritivo para login
      auth: rateLimit({
        store: new RedisStore({
          client: this.redisClient,
          prefix: 'rl:auth:'
        }),
        windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
        max: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_MAX_LOGIN_ATTEMPTS) || 5,
        message: {
          error: 'Too many login attempts',
          retryAfter: '15 minutes',
          blocked: true
        },
        skipSuccessfulRequests: true, // Não contar tentativas bem-sucedidas
        keyGenerator: (req) => {
          const ip = req.ip;
          const identifier = req.body.email || req.body.username || 'unknown';
          return `auth:${ip}:${identifier}`;
        }
      }),

      // Limiter específico para LLM (prevenir abuso de custo)
      llm: rateLimit({
        store: new RedisStore({
          client: this.redisClient,
          prefix: 'rl:llm:'
        }),
        windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, // 1 hora
        max: 100, // 100 requisições por hora por usuário
        message: {
          error: 'LLM rate limit exceeded',
          retryAfter: '1 hour'
        },
        keyGenerator: (req) => {
          const userId = req.user?.id || 'anonymous';
          return `llm:${userId}`;
        }
      }),

      // Limiter para WhatsApp API
      whatsapp: rateLimit({
        store: new RedisStore({
          client: this.redisClient,
          prefix: 'rl:wa:'
        }),
        windowMs: 60 * 1000, // 1 minuto
        max: parseInt(process.env.WA_MESSAGE_RATE_LIMIT) || 30,
        message: {
          error: 'WhatsApp API rate limit exceeded',
          retryAfter: '1 minute'
        }
      })
    };
  }

  // Middleware para bloquear IPs maliciosos
  async ipBlocker(req, res, next) {
    const ip = req.ip;
    const blockKey = `blocked:ip:${ip}`;
    
    try {
      const isBlocked = await this.redisClient.get(blockKey);
      if (isBlocked) {
        const blockData = JSON.parse(isBlocked);
        const remainingTime = Math.ceil((blockData.expiresAt - Date.now()) / 1000 / 60);
        
        return res.status(429).json({
          error: 'IP temporarily blocked',
          reason: blockData.reason,
          remainingMinutes: remainingTime,
          contactSupport: true
        });
      }
      next();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('IP blocker error:', error);
      next();
    }
  }

  // Método para bloquear IP manualmente (usado em incident response)
  async blockIP(ip, reason, minutes = 60) {
    const blockData = {
      ip,
      reason,
      blockedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      expiresAt: Date.now() + (minutes * 60 * 1000),
      blockedBy: 'security-system'
    };

    await this.redisClient.setex(
      `blocked:ip:${ip}`,
      minutes * 60,
      JSON.stringify(blockData)
    );

    // Log de segurança
    this.logSecurityEvent('IP_BLOCKED', blockData);
  }

  logSecurityEvent(event, data) {
    const logEntry = {
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      event,
      data,
      severity: 'HIGH'
    };

    console.log('[SECURITY]', JSON.stringify(logEntry));
    
    // Enviar para sistema de logging centralizado se configurado
    if (process.env.SECURITY_LOG_ENDPOINT) {
      fetch(process.env.SECURITY_LOG_ENDPOINT, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify(logEntry)
      }).catch(console.error);
    }
  }

  getMiddleware(type = 'api') {
    return this.rateLimiters[type] || this.rateLimiters.api;
  }
}

module.exports = new SecurityRateLimiter();
```

### 2.3 Sanitização de Inputs

**src/security/middleware/input-sanitizer.js:**
```javascript
const { body, query, param, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const { sanitize } = require('dompurify');
const { createDOMPurify } = require('dompurify');
const { JSDOM } = require('jsdom');
const xss = require('xss');

const window = new JSDOM('').window;
const DOMPurify = createDOMPurify(window);

class InputSanitizer {
  constructor() {
    this.xssOptions = {
      whiteList: {}, // Empty object means no tags are allowed
      stripIgnoreTag: true, // Strip HTML tags
      stripIgnoreTagBody: ['script', 'style'], // Strip these tags completely
      css: false // Disable CSS parsing
    };

    this.xssFilter = new xss.FilterXSS(this.xssOptions);
  }

  // Validação e sanitização genérica
  sanitizeInput() {
    return [
      // Sanitização de body
      body('*').customSanitizer((value, { path }) => {
        return this.sanitizeField(value, path);
      }),
      
      // Sanitização de query params
      query('*').customSanitizer((value, { path }) => {
        return this.sanitizeField(value, path);
      }),
      
      // Sanitização de route params
      param('*').customSanitizer((value, { path }) => {
        return this.sanitizeField(value, path);
      }),
      
      // Tratamento de erros de validação
      (req, res, next) => {
        const errors = validationResult(req);
        if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
          const sanitizedErrors = errors.array().map(err => ({
            field: err.param,
            message: this.xssFilter.process(err.msg),
            value: err.value ? this.xssFilter.process(String(err.value).substring(0, 50)) : undefined
          }));
          
          return res.status(400).json({
            error: 'Validation failed',
            details: sanitizedErrors
          });
        }
        next();
      }
    ];
  }

  sanitizeField(value, fieldPath) {
    if (value === undefined || value === null) return value;
    
    // Converter para string para sanitização
    const stringValue = String(value);
    
    // Aplicar sanitização baseada no tipo de campo
    if (this.isEmailField(fieldPath)) {
      return this.sanitizeEmail(stringValue);
    } else if (this.isPasswordField(fieldPath)) {
      return this.sanitizePassword(stringValue);
    } else if (this.isURLField(fieldPath)) {
      return this.sanitizeURL(stringValue);
    } else if (this.isTextField(fieldPath)) {
      return this.sanitizeText(stringValue);
    } else if (this.isJSONField(fieldPath)) {
      return this.sanitizeJSON(stringValue);
    } else {
      return this.sanitizeGeneric(stringValue);
    }
  }

  sanitizeEmail(email) {
    // Remover caracteres não-ASCII e limitar tamanho
    const clean = email.toLowerCase().replace(/[^\w@\.\-]/g, '').substring(0, 254);
    // Validar formato básico de email
    const emailRegex = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/;
    return emailRegex.test(clean) ? clean : '';
  }

  sanitizePassword(password) {
    // Não sanitizar senhas - apenas validar
    if (password.length < 8) throw new Error('Password must be at least 8 characters');
    if (password.length > 128) throw new Error('Password too long');
    return password; // Hash será aplicado depois
  }

  sanitizeURL(url) {
    try {
      const parsed = new URL(url);
      // Permitir apenas protocolos seguros
      if (!['http:', 'https:'].includes(parsed.protocol)) {
        throw new Error('Invalid protocol');
      }
      
      // Sanitizar partes da URL
      parsed.hostname = parsed.hostname.replace(/[^\w\.\-]/g, '');
      parsed.pathname = this.xssFilter.process(parsed.pathname);
      
      return parsed.toString();
    } catch {
      return '';
    }
  }

  sanitizeText(text) {
    // Remover caracteres de controle (exceto tab, newline, carriage return)
    let clean =

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
```python
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core
# AI Ops: Sistema de Monitoramento de Performance e Rollback Automático
# Arquitetura: Agentes de métricas + Sistema de decisão baseado em SLOs

"""
Estrutura do sistema:
- metrics_agent.py: Coleta métricas de performance (P50, P95, P99, erro rate)
- rollback_controller.py: Toma decisões de rollback baseado em SLOs
- dashboard.html: Interface de monitoramento em tempo real
- config.yaml: Configuração de SLOs e thresholds
- alert_manager.py: Sistema de notificações e alertas
"""

# =========== config.yaml ===========
"""
# Configuração de SLOs e thresholds
slo_config:
  response_time:
    p95_max_ms: 8000  # 8 segundos para LLMs
    p99_max_ms: 15000 # 15 segundos
    degradation_threshold: 1.5  # 50% pior que baseline
  
  error_rate:
    max_percentage: 1.0  # 1% máximo de erros
    window_minutes: 30   # janela de avaliação
  
  availability:
    min_percentage: 99.0  # 99% disponibilidade
    window_hours: 1
  
  cost:
    weekly_increase_threshold: 0.2  # 20%
    feature_cost_threshold: 0.4     # 40% do total

rollback_config:
  auto_rollback_enabled: true
  evaluation_interval_seconds: 60
  consecutive_violations_for_rollback: 3
  rollback_target: "previous_stable_version"
  notification_channels:
    - slack: "#alerts-ai-ops"
    - email: "ai-ops-team@company.com"
  
  providers:
    anthropic:
      fallback_to: "google_gemini"
      max_fallback_rate: 0.05  # 5%
    
    google:
      fallback_to: "anthropic_claude"
      max_fallback_rate: 0.05
    
    openai:
      fallback_to: "anthropic_claude"
      max_fallback_rate: 0.05

features_monitoring:
  - name: "document_summarization"
    expected_p95_ms: 5000
    expected_tokens_per_call: 2000
    cost_per_call_threshold_usd: 0.10
  
  - name: "code_generation"
    expected_p95_ms: 10000
    expected_tokens_per_call: 4000
    cost_per_call_threshold_usd: 0.20
  
  - name: "customer_support"
    expected_p95_ms: 3000
    expected_tokens_per_call: 1500
    cost_per_call_threshold_usd: 0.05
"""

# =========== metrics_agent.py ===========
import time
import asyncio
import statistics
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from collections import defaultdict, deque
import logging
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
import json
import psutil
import aiohttp

logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler('ai_ops_metrics.log'),
        logging.StreamHandler()
    ]
)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

@dataclass
class LLMCallMetrics:
    """Métricas de uma chamada individual de LLM"""
    timestamp: datetime
    provider: str
    model: str
    feature: str
    input_tokens: int
    output_tokens: int
    total_tokens: int
    latency_ms: float
    success: bool
    error_type: Optional[str] = None
    cost_usd: Optional[float] = None
    fallback_triggered: bool = False
    fallback_to: Optional[str] = None

@dataclass
class AggregatedMetrics:
    """Métricas agregadas por período"""
    period_start: datetime
    period_end: datetime
    provider: str
    model: str
    feature: str
    
    # Latência
    p50_latency_ms: float
    p95_latency_ms: float
    p99_latency_ms: float
    avg_latency_ms: float
    max_latency_ms: float
    
    # Taxas
    success_rate: float
    error_rate: float
    fallback_rate: float
    
    # Tokens
    avg_input_tokens: float
    avg_output_tokens: float
    total_tokens: int
    
    # Custo
    total_cost_usd: float
    avg_cost_per_call_usd: float
    
    # Volume
    total_calls: int
    successful_calls: int
    failed_calls: int

class MetricsAgent:
    """Agente de coleta e agregação de métricas de performance"""
    
    def __init__(self, config_path: str = "config.yaml"):
        self.config = self._load_config(config_path)
        self.metrics_buffer: List[LLMCallMetrics] = []
        self.aggregated_metrics: Dict[str, List[AggregatedMetrics]] = defaultdict(list)
        
        # Janelas deslizantes para cálculos em tempo real
        self.response_times: Dict[str, deque] = defaultdict(lambda: deque(maxlen=1000))
        self.error_counts: Dict[str, deque] = defaultdict(lambda: deque(maxlen=100))
        
        # Baseline dinâmica
        self.baseline_metrics: Dict[str, Dict] = defaultdict(dict)
        
        # Conexão com LLM Gateway
        self.gateway_url = "http://llm-gateway:8080"
        
        logger.info("Metrics Agent inicializado")
    
    def _load_config(self, config_path: str) -> Dict:
        """Carrega configuração do arquivo YAML"""
        import yaml
        try:
            with open(config_path, 'r') as f:
                return yaml.safe_load(f)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            logger.warning(f"Config file {config_path} not found, using defaults")
            return {
                "aggregation_interval_seconds": 60,
                "retention_days": 90,
                "real_time_window_minutes": 5
            }
    
    async def record_llm_call(self, metrics: LLMCallMetrics):
        """Registra uma chamada de LLM no buffer"""
        self.metrics_buffer.append(metrics)
        
        # Atualiza janelas deslizantes
        key = f"{metrics.provider}:{metrics.feature}"
        self.response_times[key].append(metrics.latency_ms)
        self.error_counts[key].append(0 if metrics.success else 1)
        
        # Se buffer cheio, processa
        if len(self.metrics_buffer) >= 100:
            await self._process_buffer()
    
    async def _process_buffer(self):
        """Processa buffer de métricas e agrega"""
        if not self.metrics_buffer:
            return
        
        # Agrupa por provider, model e feature
        grouped = defaultdict(list)
        for metric in self.metrics_buffer:
            key = f"{metric.provider}:{metric.model}:{metric.feature}"
            grouped[key].append(metric)
        
        # Calcula métricas agregadas
        now = datetime.now()
        period_start = now - timedelta(seconds=self.config.get("aggregation_interval_seconds", 60))
        
        for key, metrics_list in grouped.items():
            provider, model, feature = key.split(":")
            
            latencies = [m.latency_ms for m in metrics_list]
            successes = [m.success for m in metrics_list]
            input_tokens = [m.input_tokens for m in metrics_list]
            output_tokens = [m.output_tokens for m in metrics_list]
            costs = [m.cost_usd or 0 for m in metrics_list]
            fallbacks = [m.fallback_triggered for m in metrics_list]
            
            aggregated = AggregatedMetrics(
                period_start=period_start,
                period_end=now,
                provider=provider,
                model=model,
                feature=feature,
                p50_latency_ms=statistics.quantiles(latencies, n=100)[49] if len(latencies) >= 5 else 0,
                p95_latency_ms=statistics.quantiles(latencies, n=100)[94] if len(latencies) >= 20 else 0,
                p99_latency_ms=statistics.quantiles(latencies, n=100)[98] if len(latencies) >= 100 else 0,
                avg_latency_ms=statistics.mean(latencies) if latencies else 0,
                max_latency_ms=max(latencies) if latencies else 0,
                success_rate=sum(successes) / len(successes) if successes else 1.0,
                error_rate=1 - (sum(successes) / len(successes)) if successes else 0.0,
                fallback_rate=sum(fallbacks) / len(fallbacks) if fallbacks else 0.0,
                avg_input_tokens=statistics.mean(input_tokens) if input_tokens else 0,
                avg_output_tokens=statistics.mean(output_tokens) if output_tokens else 0,
                total_tokens=sum(m.total_tokens for m in metrics_list),
                total_cost_usd=sum(costs),
                avg_cost_per_call_usd=statistics.mean(costs) if costs else 0,
                total_calls=len(metrics_list),
                successful_calls=sum(successes),
                failed_calls=len(successes) - sum(successes)
            )
            
            self.aggregated_metrics[key].append(aggregated)
            
            # Mantém apenas 90 dias de histórico
            cutoff = now - timedelta(days=self.config.get("retention_days", 90))
            self.aggregated_metrics[key] = [
                m for m in self.aggregated_metrics[key] 
                if m.period_end > cutoff
            ]
        
        # Limpa buffer
        self.metrics_buffer.clear()
        
        logger.info(f"Processadas {len(grouped)} grupos de métricas")
    
    def get_realtime_metrics(self, provider: str = None, feature: str = None) -> Dict:
        """Retorna métricas em tempo real (últimos 5 minutos)"""
        metrics = {}
        
        for key in self.response_times:
            prov, feat = key.split(":")
            
            if provider and prov != provider:
                continue
            if feature and feat != feature:
                continue
            
            latencies = list(self.response_times[key])
            errors = list(self.error_counts[key])
            
            if latencies:
                metrics[key] = {
                    "p50_latency_ms": statistics.quantiles(latencies, n=100)[49] if len(latencies) >= 5 else 0,
                    "p95_latency_ms": statistics.quantiles(latencies, n=100)[94] if len(latencies) >= 20 else 0,
                    "p99_latency_ms": statistics.quantiles(latencies, n=100)[98] if len(latencies) >= 100 else 0,
                    "error_rate": statistics.mean(errors) if errors else 0.0,
                    "call_rate_per_minute": len(latencies) / self.config.get("real_time_window_minutes", 5),
                    "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
                }
        
        return metrics
    
    def calculate_baseline(self, days: int = 7) -> Dict[str, Dict]:
        """Calcula baseline histórica dos últimos N dias"""
        now = datetime.now()
        cutoff = now - timedelta(days=days)
        
        baseline = {}
        
        for key, metrics_list in self.aggregated_metrics.items():
            recent_metrics = [
                m for m in metrics_list 
                if m.period_end > cutoff
            ]
            
            if not recent_metrics:
                continue
            
            provider, model, feature = key.split(":")
            
            baseline[key] = {
                "p95_latency_ms": statistics.mean([m.p95_latency_ms for m in recent_metrics]),
                "p99_latency_ms": statistics.mean([m.p99_latency_ms for m in recent_metrics]),
                "error_rate": statistics.mean([m.error_rate for m in recent_metrics]),
                "success_rate": statistics.mean([m.success_rate for m in recent_metrics]),
                "avg_cost_per_call_usd": statistics.mean([m.avg_cost_per_call_usd for m in recent_metrics]),
                "calls_per_day": len(recent_metrics) / days,
                "calculated_at": now.isoformat(),
                "days_considered": days
            }
        
        self.baseline_metrics = baseline
        logger.info(f"Baseline calculada para {len(baseline)} chaves")
        
        return baseline
    
    def detect_anomalies(self) -> List[Dict]:
        """Detecta anomalias comparando com baseline e SLOs"""
        anomalies = []
        now = datetime.now()
        
        # Verifica SLOs de latência
        slo_config = self.config.get("slo_config", {})
        rt_config = slo_config.get("response_time", {})
        
        for key, realtime in self.get_realtime_metrics().items():
            provider, feature = key.split(":")
            
            # Verifica P95 vs SLO
            p95_max = rt_config.get("p95_max_ms", 8000)
            if realtime.get("p95_latency_ms", 0) > p95_max:
                anomalies.append({
                    "type": "SLO_VIOLATION",
                    "severity": "HIGH",
                    "metric": "p95_latency_ms",
                    "value": realtime["p95_latency_ms"],
                    "threshold": p95_max,
                    "provider": provider,
                    "feature": feature,
                    "timestamp": now.isoformat(),
                    "message": f"P95 latency {realtime['p95_latency_ms']:.0f}ms exceeds SLO of {p95_max}ms"
                })
            
            # Verifica degradação vs baseline
            baseline = self.baseline_metrics.get(key, {})
            if baseline and "p95_latency_ms" in baseline:
                degradation_threshold = rt_config.get("degradation_threshold", 1.5)
                current_p95 = realtime.get("p95_latency_ms", 0)
                baseline_p95 = baseline["p95_latency_ms"]
                
                if baseline_p95 > 0 and current_p95 > baseline_p95 * degradation_threshold:
                    anomalies.append({
                        "type": "PERFORMANCE_DEGRADATION",
                        "severity": "MEDIUM",
                        "metric": "p95_latency_ms",
                        "value": current_p95,
                        "baseline": baseline_p95,
                        "degradation_percent": ((current_p95 - baseline_p95) / baseline_p95) * 100,
                        "provider": provider,
                        "feature": feature,
                        "timestamp": now.isoformat(),
                        "message": f"P95 latency degraded {((current_p95 - baseline_p95) / baseline_p95) * 100:.1f}% vs baseline"
                    })
            
            # Verifica taxa de erro
            error_config = slo_config.get("error_rate", {})
            max_error_rate = error_config.get("max_percentage", 1.0) / 100
            current_error_rate = realtime.get("error_rate", 0)
            
            if current_error_rate > max_error_rate:
                anomalies.append({
                    "type": "ERROR_RATE_VIOLATION",
                    "severity": "HIGH",
                    "metric": "error_rate",
                    "value": current_error_rate * 100,
                    "threshold": max_error_rate * 100,
                    "provider": provider,
                    "feature": feature,
                    "timestamp": now.isoformat(),
                    "message": f"Error rate {current_error_rate*100:.1f}% exceeds threshold of {max_error_rate*100:.1f}%"
                })
        
        return anomalies
    
    async def start_periodic_processing(self):
        """Inicia processamento periódico de métricas"""
        interval = self.config.get("aggregation_interval_seconds", 60)
        
        while True:
            try:
                await self._process_buffer()
                await asyncio.sleep(interval)
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Erro no processamento periódico: {e}")
                await asyncio.sleep(5)

# =========== rollback_controller.py ===========
import asyncio
from enum import Enum
from typing import Dict, List, Optional
import yaml
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import subprocess
import docker
from dataclasses import dataclass
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class RollbackDecision(Enum):
    NO_ACTION = "no_action"
    TRIGGER_FALLBACK = "trigger_fallback"
    ROLLBACK_VERSION = "rollback_version"
    NOTIFY_ONLY = "notify_only"
    SCALE_RESOURCES = "scale_resources"

@dataclass
class ViolationRecord:
    """Registro de violação de SLO"""
    timestamp: datetime
    violation_type: str
    provider: str
    feature: str
    metric: str
    value: float
    threshold: float
    severity: str

class RollbackController:
    """Controlador de rollback automático baseado em métricas"""
    
    def __init__(self, metrics_agent: MetricsAgent, config_path: str = "config.yaml"):
        self.metrics_agent = metrics_agent
        self.config = self._load_config(config_path)
        self.violation_history: Dict[str, List[ViolationRecord]] = defaultdict(list)
        self.rollback_state: Dict[str, Dict] = defaultdict(dict)
        
        # Estado dos provedores
        self.provider_states = {
            "anthropic": {"healthy": True, "fallback_count": 0, "last_fallback": None},
            "google": {"healthy": True, "fallback_count": 0, "last_fallback": None},
            "openai": {"healthy": True, "fallback_count": 0,

## 1. Documento Principal: V10_ARCHITECTURE_OVERVIEW.md

```markdown
# DIYAPP V10 - Arquitetura de Referência
**Data de criação:** 2024-01-15  
**Última atualização:** 2024-01-15  
**Owner:** Tech Lead  
**Status:** Ativo

## Visão Geral
A V10 do DIYAPP representa uma reestruturação completa para atingir 100% de estabilidade autônoma usando o Modo Hive para refatoração paralela.

### Componentes Principais

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    Load Balancer (HAProxy)                  │
└─────────────────┬───────────────────┬───────────────────────┘
                  │                   │
    ┌─────────────▼──────┐   ┌───────▼──────────────┐
    │   API Gateway      │   │   WebSocket Hub      │
    │   (Rate Limiting)  │   │   (Real-time)        │
    └─────────┬──────────┘   └──────────┬───────────┘
              │                          │
    ┌─────────▼──────────────────────────▼──────────┐
    │           Service Mesh (V10 Core)             │
    │  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐    │
    │  │ Auth     │  │ Data     │  │ Queue    │    │
    │  │ Service  │  │ Service  │  │ Service  │    │
    │  └──────────┘  └──────────┘  └──────────┘    │
    └─────────────────┬─────────────────────────────┘
                      │
          ┌───────────▼─────────────┐
          │   Database Layer        │
          │  ┌─────┐  ┌──────────┐  │
          │  │ PG  │  │ Redis    │  │
          │  │     │  │ Cluster  │  │
          │  └─────┘  └──────────┘  │
          └──────────────────────────┘
```

## Modo Hive - Refatoração Paralela

### Estrutura de Implantação
```
Legacy V9 ───┐
             ├──▶ Hive Controller ───▶ V10 Canary (5%)
V10 Alpha ───┘                        V10 Stable (95%)
```

### Regras de Transição
1. **Fase 1 (0-30 dias):** 5% do tráfego para V10
2. **Fase 2 (31-60 dias):** 50% do tráfego para V10
3. **Fase 3 (61+ dias):** 100% do tráfego para V10

## Requisitos de Estabilidade

### SLAs por Componente
| Componente | Disponibilidade | Latência P95 | Throughput |
|------------|----------------|--------------|------------|
| API Gateway | 99.99% | <100ms | 10k RPM |
| Auth Service | 99.95% | <50ms | 5k RPM |
| Data Service | 99.99% | <200ms | 20k RPM |
| WebSocket | 99.9% | <10ms | 50k conexões |

### Circuit Breakers
```yaml
circuit_breakers:
  api_gateway:
    failure_threshold: 5
    timeout: 3000ms
    reset_timeout: 30000ms
  data_service:
    failure_threshold: 3
    timeout: 5000ms
    reset_timeout: 60000ms
```

## Monitoramento
- **Métricas:** Prometheus + Grafana
- **Logs:** ELK Stack (Elasticsearch, Logstash, Kibana)
- **Tracing:** Jaeger para distributed tracing
- **Alertas:** PagerDuty integrado com runbooks

---
**Próxima revisão:** 2024-02-15  
**Responsável pela atualização:** Tech Lead
```

## 2. Documento de API: OPENAPI_SPEC.yaml

```yaml
openapi: 3.0.0
info:
  title: DIYAPP V10 API
  version: 10.0.0
  description: |
    API principal do DIYAPP V10 com suporte a funcionalidades premium.
    **Breaking Changes da V9:**
    - Autenticação migrada para JWT Bearer tokens
    - Todos os endpoints requerem API-Version header
    - Paginação obrigatória em listagens
  contact:
    name: Suporte DIYAPP
    email: api-support@diyapp.com
  license:
    name: Proprietário
    url: https://diyapp.com/terms

servers:
  - url: https://api.diyapp.com/v10
    description: Produção
  - url: https://api-staging.diyapp.com/v10
    description: Staging
  - url: http://localhost:3000/v10
    description: Desenvolvimento local

tags:
  - name: Autenticação
    description: Login, logout e gestão de tokens
  - name: Usuários
    description: Operações de perfil de usuário
  - name: Projetos Premium
    description: Funcionalidades exclusivas para planos premium
  - name: Templates
    description: Templates e modelos pré-configurados

paths:
  /auth/login:
    post:
      tags: [Autenticação]
      summary: Login de usuário
      description: Autentica um usuário e retorna tokens JWT
      operationId: loginUser
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/LoginRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Login bem-sucedido
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/LoginResponse'
        '401':
          description: Credenciais inválidas
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'
        '429':
          description: Muitas tentativas de login
          
  /users/{userId}/projects:
    get:
      tags: [Projetos Premium]
      summary: Listar projetos do usuário
      description: Retorna projetos com filtros avançados (apenas premium)
      operationId: listUserProjects
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - name: userId
          in: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
          description: ID do usuário
        - name: filter
          in: query
          required: false
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [active, archived, template]
          description: Filtro de status
        - name: page
          in: query
          required: true
          schema:
            type: integer
            minimum: 1
            default: 1
        - name: limit
          in: query
          required: true
          schema:
            type: integer
            minimum: 1
            maximum: 100
            default: 20
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Lista de projetos
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/ProjectList'
        '403':
          description: Plano free - upgrade necessário para filtros
          
  /premium/templates/{templateId}/instantiate:
    post:
      tags: [Templates]
      summary: Instanciar template premium
      description: Cria um novo projeto a partir de um template premium
      operationId: instantiatePremiumTemplate
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - name: templateId
          in: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/TemplateInstantiation'
      responses:
        '201':
          description: Template instanciado com sucesso
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Project'
        '402':
          description: Créditos insuficientes
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'

components:
  securitySchemes:
    bearerAuth:
      type: http
      scheme: bearer
      bearerFormat: JWT
    apiKey:
      type: apiKey
      in: header
      name: X-API-Key
      
  schemas:
    LoginRequest:
      type: object
      required:
        - email
        - password
      properties:
        email:
          type: string
          format: email
          example: usuario@exemplo.com
        password:
          type: string
          format: password
          example: "senha123"
        twoFactorCode:
          type: string
          description: Código 2FA (opcional)
          
    LoginResponse:
      type: object
      properties:
        accessToken:
          type: string
          description: Token JWT para autenticação
          example: "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9..."
        refreshToken:
          type: string
          description: Token para renovar acesso
        expiresIn:
          type: integer
          description: Segundos até expiração
          example: 3600
        user:
          $ref: '#/components/schemas/User'
          
    Project:
      type: object
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
          format: uuid
        name:
          type: string
        type:
          type: string
          enum: [basic, premium, enterprise]
        createdAt:
          type: string
          format: date-time
        updatedAt:
          type: string
          format: date-time
        metadata:
          type: object
          additionalProperties: true
          
    Error:
      type: object
      properties:
        error:
          type: string
          example: "invalid_credentials"
        message:
          type: string
          example: "As credenciais fornecidas são inválidas"
        details:
          type: object
          additionalProperties: true
        timestamp:
          type: string
          format: date-time
```

## 3. Guia de Implantação: DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE.md

```markdown
# Guia de Implantação - DIYAPP V10
**Data de criação:** 2024-01-15  
**Última atualização:** 2024-01-15  
**Owner:** SRE

## Pré-requisitos

### Infraestrutura Mínima
- Kubernetes 1.24+ ou Docker Swarm
- 4 CPUs, 16GB RAM (mínimo)
- PostgreSQL 14+ com replicação
- Redis 7+ Cluster
- 50GB de armazenamento

### Variáveis de Ambiente Críticas
```bash
# Banco de dados
export DB_HOST=postgres-primary
export DB_PORT=5432
export DB_NAME=diyapp_v10
export DB_USER=diyapp_user

# Redis
export REDIS_NODES="redis-node-1:6379,redis-node-2:6379,redis-node-3:6379"

# Segurança
export JWT_SECRET=$(openssl rand -base64 64)
export ENCRYPTION_KEY=$(openssl rand -base64 32)

# Modo Hive
export HIVE_MODE_ENABLED=true
export TRAFFIC_PERCENTAGE=5  # Inicia com 5% do tráfego
```

## Implantação com Kubernetes

### 1. Namespace e Configurações
```yaml
# namespace.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Namespace
metadata:
  name: diyapp-v10
  labels:
    app: diyapp
    version: v10
    stability: canary
```

### 2. ConfigMap para Variáveis
```yaml
# configmap.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: diyapp-v10-config
  namespace: diyapp-v10
data:
  APP_ENV: production
  LOG_LEVEL: info
  HIVE_CONTROLLER_ENDPOINT: http://hive-controller:8080
  CANARY_ENABLED: "true"
```

### 3. Deployment Principal
```yaml
# deployment.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: diyapp-v10-core
  namespace: diyapp-v10
  labels:
    app: diyapp
    version: v10
    component: core
spec:
  replicas: 3
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxSurge: 1
      maxUnavailable: 0
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: diyapp
      version: v10
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: diyapp
        version: v10
        component: core
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: api
        image: diyapp/v10-core:1.0.0
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3000
          name: http
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /ready
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "512Mi"
            cpu: "250m"
          limits:
            memory: "1Gi"
            cpu: "500m"
        envFrom:
        - configMapRef:
            name: diyapp-v10-config
        env:
        - name: POD_NAME
          valueFrom:
            fieldRef:
              fieldPath: metadata.name
        - name: JWT_SECRET
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: diyapp-secrets
              key: jwt-secret
```

### 4. Service e Ingress
```yaml
# service.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: diyapp-v10-service
  namespace: diyapp-v10
  annotations:
    service.beta.kubernetes.io/aws-load-balancer-type: "nlb"
spec:
  selector:
    app: diyapp
    version: v10
  ports:
  - port: 80
    targetPort: 3000
    name: http
  - port: 443
    targetPort: 3000
    name: https
  type: LoadBalancer

# ingress.yaml
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  name: diyapp-v10-ingress
  namespace: diyapp-v10
  annotations:
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/rewrite-target: /
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/ssl-redirect: "true"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/canary: "true"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/canary-weight: "5"
spec:
  ingressClassName: nginx
  tls:
  - hosts:
    - api.diyapp.com
    secretName: diyapp-tls
  rules:
  - host: api.diyapp.com
    http:
      paths:
      - path: /v10
        pathType: Prefix
        backend:
          service:
            name: diyapp-v10-service
            port:
              number: 80
```

## Implantação com Docker Compose (Desenvolvimento)

```yaml
# docker-compose.v10.yml
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:14-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_v10
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  api:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.api
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: development

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Sistema de Monitoramento e Rollback Automático

Vou implementar um sistema completo de monitoramento de performance com métricas P95 e sistema de rollback automático baseado em thresholds pré-definidos.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-monitoring/
├── src/
│   ├── monitoring/
│   │   ├── agent.js
│   │   ├── metrics-collector.js
│   │   ├── rollback-controller.js
│   │   └── alert-manager.js

## 3. Agente de Monitoramento (src/monitoring/agent.js)

```javascript
const EventEmitter = require('events');
const winston = require('winston');
const path = require('path');

class MonitoringAgent extends EventEmitter {
  constructor(config) {
    super();
    this.config = config;
    this.metrics = {
      responseTimes: [],
      errorCount: 0,
      requestCount: 0,
      startTime: Date.now()
    };
    
    this.setupLogger();
    this.setupCleanupInterval();
  }

  setupLogger() {
    this.logger = winston.createLogger({
      level: 'info',
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.timestamp(),
        winston.format.json()
      ),
      transports: [
        new winston.transports.File({ 
          filename: path.join(__dirname, '../../logs/monitoring.log'),
          maxsize: 5242880,
          maxFiles: 5
        }),
        new winston.transports.Console({
          format: winston.format.simple()
        })
      ]
    });
  }

  setupCleanupInterval() {
    setInterval(() => {
      const retentionPeriod = this.config.metrics.retentionPeriod;
      const cutoff = Date.now() - retentionPeriod;
      
      this.metrics.responseTimes = this.metrics.responseTimes.filter(
        metric => metric.timestamp > cutoff
      );
    }, 60000);
  }

  recordResponseTime(duration, endpoint, method, statusCode) {
    const metric = {
      duration,
      endpoint,
      method,
      statusCode,
      timestamp: Date.now()
    };

    this.metrics.responseTimes.push(metric);
    this.metrics.requestCount++;

    if (statusCode >= 400) {
      this.metrics.errorCount++;
      this.emit('error', {
        endpoint,
        statusCode,
        duration,
        timestamp: metric.timestamp
      });
    }

    this.emit('metric', metric);
    
    // Verificar thresholds em tempo real
    this.checkThresholds();
  }

  calculatePercentiles(percentiles) {
    if (this.metrics.responseTimes.length === 0) {
      return {};
    }

    const durations = this.metrics.responseTimes
      .slice(-1000) // Últimos 1000 requests para cálculo
      .map(m => m.duration)
      .sort((a, b) => a - b);

    const results = {};
    percentiles.forEach(p => {
      const index = Math.ceil(p * durations.length) - 1;
      results[`p${p * 100}`] = durations[Math.max(0, index)];
    });

    return results;
  }

  calculateErrorRate() {
    if (this.metrics.requestCount === 0) return 0;
    return this.metrics.errorCount / this.metrics.requestCount;
  }

  getCurrentMetrics() {
    const percentiles = this.calculatePercentiles(this.config.metrics.percentiles);
    const uptime = Date.now() - this.metrics.startTime;
    
    return {
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      requestCount: this.metrics.requestCount,
      errorCount: this.metrics.errorCount,
      errorRate: this.calculateErrorRate(),
      responseTimePercentiles: percentiles,
      currentResponseTimes: this.metrics.responseTimes.slice(-10),
      uptime,
      throughput: this.metrics.requestCount / (uptime / 1000)
    };
  }

  checkThresholds() {
    const metrics = this.getCurrentMetrics();
    const thresholds = this.config.thresholds;
    const violations = [];

    // Verificar P95
    if (metrics.responseTimePercentiles.p95 > thresholds.responseTimeP95) {
      violations.push({
        metric: 'responseTimeP95',
        value: metrics.responseTimePercentiles.p95,
        threshold: thresholds.responseTimeP95,
        severity: 'high'
      });
    }

    // Verificar taxa de erro
    if (metrics.errorRate > thresholds.errorRate) {
      violations.push({
        metric: 'errorRate',
        value: metrics.errorRate,
        threshold: thresholds.errorRate,
        severity: 'critical'
      });
    }

    if (violations.length > 0) {
      this.emit('thresholdViolation', {
        violations,
        timestamp: Date.now(),
        metrics
      });
      
      this.logger.warn('Threshold violations detected', { violations });
    }
  }

  resetMetrics() {
    this.metrics = {
      responseTimes: [],
      errorCount: 0,
      requestCount: 0,
      startTime: Date.now()
    };
  }
}

module.exports = MonitoringAgent;
```

## 4. Coletor de Métricas do Sistema (src/monitoring/metrics-collector.js)

```javascript
const os = require('os');
const { exec } = require('child_process');
const util = require('util');
const execPromise = util.promisify(exec);

class SystemMetricsCollector {
  constructor() {
    this.metrics = {
      cpu: { usage: 0, loadAverage: [0, 0, 0] },
      memory: { used: 0, total: 0, free: 0, percentage: 0 },
      disk: { used: 0, total: 0, free: 0, percentage: 0 },
      network: { rx: 0, tx: 0 }
    };
    
    this.previousNetworkStats = this.getNetworkStats();
    this.collectionInterval = null;
  }

  async collectAllMetrics() {
    await Promise.all([
      this.collectCpuMetrics(),
      this.collectMemoryMetrics(),
      this.collectDiskMetrics(),
      this.collectNetworkMetrics()
    ]);
    
    return this.metrics;
  }

  async collectCpuMetrics() {
    const cpus = os.cpus();
    let totalIdle = 0, totalTick = 0;
    
    cpus.forEach(cpu => {
      for (let type in cpu.times) {
        totalTick += cpu.times[type];
      }
      totalIdle += cpu.times.idle;
    });
    
    const loadAverage = os.loadavg();
    this.metrics.cpu = {
      usage: ((totalTick - totalIdle) / totalTick) * 100,
      loadAverage: loadAverage,
      cores: cpus.length
    };
  }

  collectMemoryMetrics() {
    const total = os.totalmem();
    const free = os.freemem();
    const used = total - free;
    
    this.metrics.memory = {
      used: this.bytesToGB(used),
      total: this.bytesToGB(total),
      free: this.bytesToGB(free),
      percentage: (used / total) * 100
    };
  }

  async collectDiskMetrics() {
    try {
      const { stdout } = await execPromise('df -k /');
      const lines = stdout.trim().split('\n');
      const data = lines[1].split(/\s+/);
      
      const total = parseInt(data[1]) * 1024;
      const used = parseInt(data[2]) * 1024;
      const free = parseInt(data[3]) * 1024;
      
      this.metrics.disk = {
        used: this.bytesToGB(used),
        total: this.bytesToGB(total),
        free: this.bytesToGB(free),
        percentage: (used / total) * 100
      };
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error collecting disk metrics:', error);
    }
  }

  getNetworkStats() {
    const interfaces = os.networkInterfaces();
    let rx = 0, tx = 0;
    
    Object.values(interfaces).forEach(iface => {
      iface.forEach(entry => {
        if (!entry.internal) {
          rx += entry.rx_bytes || 0;
          tx += entry.tx_bytes || 0;
        }
      });
    });
    
    return { rx, tx };
  }

  collectNetworkMetrics() {
    const currentStats = this.getNetworkStats();
    const timeDiff = 1000; // 1 second
    
    const rxRate = (currentStats.rx - this.previousNetworkStats.rx) / timeDiff;
    const txRate = (currentStats.tx - this.previousNetworkStats.tx) / timeDiff;
    
    this.metrics.network = {
      rx: this.bytesToMB(rxRate),
      tx: this.bytesToMB(txRate),
      totalRx: this.bytesToGB(currentStats.rx),
      totalTx: this.bytesToGB(currentStats.tx)
    };
    
    this.previousNetworkStats = currentStats;
  }

  bytesToGB(bytes) {
    return bytes / (1024 * 1024 * 1024);
  }

  bytesToMB(bytes) {
    return bytes / (1024 * 1024);
  }

  startContinuousCollection(interval = 5000) {
    if (this.collectionInterval) {
      clearInterval(this.collectionInterval);
    }
    
    this.collectionInterval = setInterval(async () => {
      await this.collectAllMetrics();
    }, interval);
  }

  stopCollection() {
    if (this.collectionInterval) {
      clearInterval(this.collectionInterval);
      this.collectionInterval = null;
    }
  }

  getCurrentMetrics() {
    return {
      ...this.metrics,
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      hostname: os.hostname(),
      platform: os.platform(),
      uptime: os.uptime()
    };
  }
}

module.exports = SystemMetricsCollector;
```

## 5. Controlador de Rollback Automático (src/monitoring/rollback-controller.js)

```javascript
const EventEmitter = require('events');
const fs = require('fs').promises;
const path = require('path');
const { exec } = require('child_process');
const util = require('util');
const execPromise = util.promisify(exec);

class RollbackController extends EventEmitter {
  constructor(config, monitoringAgent) {
    super();
    this.config = config.rollback;
    this.monitoringAgent = monitoringAgent;
    this.violationHistory = [];
    this.rollbackHistory = [];
    this.currentVersion = null;
    this.stableVersion = null;
    
    this.loadCurrentVersion();
    this.setupMonitoringListeners();
    this.startHealthChecks();
  }

  async loadCurrentVersion() {
    try {
      const versionPath = path.join(__dirname, '../../version.json');
      const versionData = await fs.readFile(versionPath, 'utf8');
      const versionInfo = JSON.parse(versionData);
      
      this.currentVersion = versionInfo.version;
      this.stableVersion = versionInfo.stableVersion || this.currentVersion;
      
      this.log(`Current version: ${this.currentVersion}, Stable version: ${this.stableVersion}`);
    } catch (error) {
      this.log(`Error loading version: ${error.message}`);
      this.currentVersion = 'unknown';
      this.stableVersion = 'unknown';
    }
  }

  setupMonitoringListeners() {
    this.monitoringAgent.on('thresholdViolation', (data) => {
      this.handleThresholdViolation(data);
    });

    this.monitoringAgent.on('error', (error) => {
      this.recordError(error);
    });
  }

  startHealthChecks() {
    setInterval(async () => {
      await this.performHealthCheck();
    }, this.config.checkInterval);
  }

  async performHealthCheck() {
    try {
      const healthEndpoint = `${this.config.healthBaseUrl || 'http://localhost:3000'}/health`;
      const response = await fetch(healthEndpoint, { timeout: 5000 });
      
      if (!response.ok) {
        this.recordHealthCheckFailure({
          endpoint: healthEndpoint,
          status: response.status,
          timestamp: Date.now()
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      this.recordHealthCheckFailure({
        endpoint: healthEndpoint,
        error: error.message,
        timestamp: Date.now()
      });
    }
  }

  handleThresholdViolation(violationData) {
    const now = Date.now();
    this.violationHistory.push({
      ...violationData,
      recordedAt: now
    });

    // Manter apenas violações recentes
    const cutoff = now - this.config.violationDuration;
    this.violationHistory = this.violationHistory.filter(
      v => v.recordedAt > cutoff
    );

    // Verificar se devemos acionar rollback
    if (this.shouldTriggerRollback()) {
      this.triggerRollback();
    }
  }

  shouldTriggerRollback() {
    if (!this.config.enabled) return false;
    
    // Verificar limite de rollbacks por hora
    const oneHourAgo = Date.now() - 3600000;
    const recentRollbacks = this.rollbackHistory.filter(
      r => r.timestamp > oneHourAgo
    );
    
    if (recentRollbacks.length >= this.config.maxRollbacksPerHour) {
      this.log(`Max rollbacks per hour reached: ${recentRollbacks.length}`);
      return false;
    }

    // Verificar violações críticas
    const criticalViolations = this.violationHistory.filter(
      v => v.violations.some(viol => viol.severity === 'critical')
    );

    if (criticalViolations.length >= 2) {
      return true;
    }

    // Verificar múltiplas violações de alta severidade
    const highSeverityViolations = this.violationHistory.filter(
      v => v.violations.some(viol => viol.severity === 'high')
    );

    return highSeverityViolations.length >= 3;
  }

  async triggerRollback() {
    try {
      this.log(`Initiating automatic rollback from ${this.currentVersion}`);
      
      const rollbackVersion = this.determineRollbackVersion();
      
      if (!rollbackVersion) {
        throw new Error('No suitable rollback version available');
      }

      const rollbackData = {
        fromVersion: this.currentVersion,
        toVersion: rollbackVersion,
        timestamp: Date.now(),
        reason: 'Threshold violations detected',
        violations: this.violationHistory.slice(-5)
      };

      // Executar rollback
      await this.executeRollback(rollbackVersion);
      
      // Atualizar histórico
      this.rollbackHistory.push(rollbackData);
      
      // Limpar histórico de violações
      this.violationHistory = [];
      
      // Emitir evento
      this.emit('rollbackExecuted', rollbackData);
      
      // Enviar alerta
      await this.sendRollbackAlert(rollbackData);
      
      this.log(`Rollback completed to version ${rollbackVersion}`);
      
    } catch (error) {
      this.log(`Rollback failed: ${error.message}`);
      this.emit('rollbackFailed', { error: error.message, timestamp: Date.now() });
    }
  }

  determineRollbackVersion() {
    // Priorizar versão estável
    if (this.stableVersion && this.stableVersion !== this.currentVersion) {
      return this.stableVersion;
    }
    
    // Buscar versões anteriores disponíveis
    const

## 1. V10_ARCHITECTURE.md
```markdown
# DIYAPP V10 - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

## Visão Geral
**Data de Criação:** 2024-01-15  
**Última Atualização:** 2024-01-15  
**Owner:** Tech Lead  
**Status:** Ativo

## Decisões Arquiteturais (ADRs)

### ADR-001: Migração para Arquitetura de Microsserviços
**Contexto:** A V9 utilizava arquitetura monolítica que limitava escalabilidade e deploy independente.

**Decisão:** Adotar arquitetura baseada em microsserviços com os seguintes serviços:
1. **Auth Service** - Autenticação e autorização
2. **User Service** - Gestão de perfis de usuário
3. **Project Service** - Gerenciamento de projetos DIY
4. **AI Service** - Processamento de IA e recomendações
5. **Payment Service** - Processamento de pagamentos premium
6. **Notification Service** - Notificações em tempo real

**Consequências:**
- ✅ Escalabilidade independente por serviço
- ✅ Deploy contínuo sem downtime
- ✅ Resiliência a falhas isoladas
- ⚠️ Complexidade aumentada de operação
- ⚠️ Necessidade de orquestração de containers

### ADR-002: Comunicação entre Serviços
**Decisão:** Utilizar gRPC para comunicação síncrona entre serviços e RabbitMQ para mensageria assíncrona.

**Justificativa:** gRPC oferece melhor performance para chamadas síncronas, enquanto RabbitMQ garante entrega confiável de eventos.

### ADR-003: Banco de Dados por Serviço
**Decisão:** Cada serviço possui seu próprio banco de dados PostgreSQL isolado.

**Padrão Implementado:**
```sql
-- Exemplo: Schema do User Service
CREATE TABLE users (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    tier VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'free',
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Exemplo: Schema do Project Service  
CREATE TABLE projects (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id UUID NOT NULL,
    title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    complexity VARCHAR(50),
    estimated_hours INTEGER,
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'draft'
);
```

## Diagrama de Arquitetura

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    Load Balancer (NGINX)                    │
└────────────────┬────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                 │
    ┌────────────┼────────────┐
    │            │            │
┌───▼───┐  ┌────▼────┐  ┌────▼────┐
│  Web  │  │   API   │  │  Admin  │
│  App  │  │ Gateway │  │  Panel  │
└───┬───┘  └────┬────┘  └────┬────┘
    │           │            │
    └───────────┼────────────┘
                │
        ┌───────▼───────┐
        │ Service Mesh  │
        │   (Istio)     │
        └───────┬───────┘
                │
    ┌───────────┼──────────────────────────┐
    │           │                          │
┌───▼───┐  ┌───▼───┐  ┌───▼───┐  ┌───────▼───────┐
│ Auth  │  │ User  │  │Project│  │     AI        │
│Service│  │Service│  │Service│  │   Service     │
└───┬───┘  └───┬───┘  └───┬───┘  └───────┬───────┘
    │          │          │              │
┌───▼───┐  ┌───▼───┐  ┌───▼───┐  ┌───────▼───────┐
│ Redis │  │  PG   │  │  PG   │  │   Pinecone    │
│ Cache │  │(Users)│  │(Proj) │  │   Vector DB   │
└───────┘  └───────┘  └───────┘  └───────────────┘
```

## Stack Tecnológico

### Backend Services
- **Linguagem:** Go 1.21 + Python 3.11 (para serviços de IA)
- **Framework:** Gin (Go), FastAPI (Python)
- **Banco de Dados:** PostgreSQL 15 + Redis 7
- **Message Queue:** RabbitMQ 3.12
- **Service Mesh:** Istio 1.19
- **API Gateway:** Kong 3.4

### Frontend
- **Framework:** React 18 + TypeScript
- **State Management:** Zustand
- **UI Library:** Chakra UI
- **Build Tool:** Vite

### Infraestrutura
- **Container Runtime:** Docker 24 + containerd
- **Orquestração:** Kubernetes 1.28
- **CI/CD:** GitHub Actions + ArgoCD
- **Monitoring:** Prometheus + Grafana + Loki
- **Logging:** ELK Stack

## Padrões de Código

### Estrutura de Serviço
```
auth-service/
├── cmd/
│   └── main.go
├── internal/
│   ├── handlers/
│   ├── models/
│   ├── repositories/
│   └── services/
├── pkg/
│   └── utils/
├── proto/
│   └── auth.proto
├── Dockerfile
├── docker-compose.yml
└── k8s/
    ├── deployment.yaml
    └── service.yaml
```

### Configuração Centralizada
```yaml
# config/config.yaml
services:
  auth:
    port: 50051
    database:
      host: ${DB_HOST}
      port: 5432
      name: auth_db
    redis:
      host: ${REDIS_HOST}
      port: 6379
    jwt:
      secret: ${JWT_SECRET}
      expiration: 24h
```

## Considerações de Segurança

1. **Autenticação:** JWT com refresh tokens
2. **Autorização:** RBAC por serviço
3. **Criptografia:** TLS 1.3 em todas as comunicações
4. **Secrets:** HashiCorp Vault para gerenciamento
5. **Rate Limiting:** Implementado no API Gateway

## Métricas de Performance
- **Latência Alvo:** < 200ms para 95% das requisições
- **Disponibilidade:** 99.95% SLA
- **Throughput:** 1000 req/seg por serviço
- **Tempo de Recuperação:** < 5 minutos

- [Deployment Guide](./DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE.md)
- [Runbook: Incident Response](./RUNBOOKS/INCIDENT_RESPONSE.md)
```

## 2. API_REFERENCE.md
```markdown
# DIYAPP V10 - API Reference

## Visão Geral
**Base URL:** `https://api.diyapp.com/v10`  
**Formato:** JSON  
**Autenticação:** Bearer Token

## Changelog
### v10.0.0 (2024-01-15)
- **Breaking Changes:** 
  - Nova estrutura de endpoints por serviço
  - Autenticação migrada para JWT com refresh tokens
  - Todos os endpoints requerem versionamento explícito
- **Novas Features:**
  - Suporte a projetos colaborativos
  - Integração com IA generativa
  - WebSocket para notificações em tempo real

## Autenticação

### Login
```http
POST /auth/login
Content-Type: application/json

{
  "email": "user@example.com",
  "password": "securepassword"
}
```

**Response:**
```json
{
  "access_token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIs...",
  "refresh_token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIs...",
  "expires_in": 3600,
  "token_type": "Bearer"
}
```

### Refresh Token
```http
POST /auth/refresh
Authorization: Bearer {refresh_token}
```

## Endpoints Principais

### User Service

#### GET /users/me
**Descrição:** Retorna informações do usuário atual

**Headers:**
```
Authorization: Bearer {access_token}
```

**Response:**
```json
{
  "id": "uuid",
  "email": "user@example.com",
  "name": "John Doe",
  "tier": "premium",
  "created_at": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",
  "projects_count": 5
}
```

#### PUT /users/profile
**Descrição:** Atualiza perfil do usuário

**Request:**
```json
{
  "name": "Updated Name",
  "avatar_url": "https://..."
}
```

### Project Service

#### POST /projects
**Descrição:** Cria novo projeto DIY

**Request:**
```json
{
  "title": "Mesa de Centro Moderna",
  "description": "Mesa com design minimalista",
  "category": "woodworking",
  "difficulty": "intermediate",
  "estimated_hours": 8,
  "materials": [
    {"name": "Madeira de Carvalho", "quantity": "2 placas"},
    {"name": "Parafusos", "quantity": "20 unidades"}
  ],
  "steps": [
    {
      "order": 1,
      "title": "Cortar madeira",
      "description": "Cortar as placas nas medidas",
      "estimated_minutes": 60
    }
  ]
}
```

**Response:**
```json
{
  "id": "project-uuid",
  "title": "Mesa de Centro Moderna",
  "slug": "mesa-de-centro-moderna",
  "status": "draft",
  "created_at": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",
  "share_url": "https://diyapp.com/projects/mesa-de-centro-moderna"
}
```

#### GET /projects/{id}/ai-suggestions
**Descrição:** Obtém sugestões de IA para melhorar o projeto (Premium)

**Headers:**
```
Authorization: Bearer {access_token}
X-API-Key: {premium_api_key}
```

**Response:**
```json
{
  "suggestions": [
    {
      "type": "material_optimization",
      "description": "Substituir madeira de carvalho por MDF para reduzir custos em 40%",
      "confidence": 0.87,
      "estimated_savings": "R$ 120,00"
    },
    {
      "type": "safety_improvement",
      "description": "Adicionar cantos arredondados para evitar acidentes",
      "confidence": 0.92
    }
  ]
}
```

### AI Service

#### POST /ai/generate-instructions
**Descrição:** Gera instruções passo a passo com IA (Premium)

**Request:**
```json
{
  "project_description": "Quero construir uma estante flutuante para livros",
  "skill_level": "beginner",
  "available_tools": ["furadeira", "serra tico-tico"],
  "budget": 300,
  "style_preference": "modern"
}
```

**Response:**
```json
{
  "instructions": [
    {
      "step": 1,
      "title": "Medir e marcar",
      "description": "Meça o espaço na parede onde a estante será instalada...",
      "duration_minutes": 30,
      "tools_needed": ["fita métrica", "lápis"],
      "materials_needed": [],
      "safety_notes": "Use óculos de proteção ao medir em altura"
    }
  ],
  "total_estimated_hours": 4,
  "total_estimated_cost": 245.50
}
```

### Payment Service

#### POST /subscriptions/upgrade
**Descrição:** Atualiza para plano premium

**Request:**
```json
{
  "plan": "premium_annual",
  "payment_method_id": "pm_1Oa..."
}
```

**Webhook Events:**
```json
{
  "event": "subscription.created",
  "data": {
    "subscription_id": "sub_1Oa...",
    "customer_id": "cus_1Oa...",
    "status": "active",
    "current_period_end": 1707945600
  }
}
```

## WebSocket API

### Conexão
```
wss://api.diyapp.com/v10/ws
```

### Eventos

#### Autenticação
```json
{
  "type": "auth",
  "token": "access_token"
}
```

#### Notificações em Tempo Real
```json
{
  "type": "notification",
  "data": {
    "id": "notif-uuid",
    "title": "Novo comentário",
    "message": "Maria comentou no seu projeto",
    "created_at": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",
    "action_url": "/projects/project-id"
  }
}
```

## Códigos de Erro

| Código | Descrição | Solução |
|--------|-----------|---------|
| 4001 | Token expirado | Use refresh token para obter novo access token |
| 4002 | Permissão insuficiente | Verifique se seu plano inclui o recurso |
| 4003 | Rate limit excedido | Aguarde 60 segundos antes de tentar novamente |
| 5001 | Serviço temporariamente indisponível | Tente novamente em alguns minutos |
| 5002 | Erro de processamento de pagamento | Verifique os dados do cartão |

## Exemplos de Código

### JavaScript/Node.js
```javascript
const DIYAPI = {
  baseURL: 'https://api.diyapp.com/v10',
  
  async createProject(projectData) {
    const response = await fetch(`${this.baseURL}/projects`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Authorization': `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('access_token')}`,
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
      },
      body: JSON.stringify(projectData)
    });
    
    if (!response.ok) {
      throw new Error(`API Error: ${response.status}`);
    }
    
    return response.json();
  }
};
```

### Python
```python
import requests

class DIYAPIClient:
    def __init__(self, access_token):
        self.base_url = "https://api.diyapp.com/v10"
        self.headers = {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {access_token}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
    
    def get_user_profile(self):
        response = requests.get(
            f"{self.base_url}/users/me",
            headers=self.headers
        )
        response.raise_for_status()
        return response.json()
```

## Rate Limiting
- Free: 100 requests/hour
- Premium: 1000 requests/hour
- Enterprise: 10000 requests/hour

## Suporte
Para problemas com a API:
1. Consulte a [documentação de erros](#códigos-de-erro)
2. Verifique o [status do sistema](https://status.diyapp.com)
3. Entre em contato: api-support@diyapp.com
```

## 3. DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE.md
```markdown
# DIYAPP V10 - Guia de Implantação

## Pré-requisitos

### Infraestrutura
- Kubernetes 1.28+
- Helm 3.12+
- Istio 1.19+
- Cert-manager para TLS
- Storage Class configurada

### Dependências
```bash
# Verificar versões
kubectl version --client
helm version
istioctl version
docker --version
```

## Configuração do Ambiente

### 1. Clone o Repositório
```bash
git clone https://github.com/diyapp/v10-core.git
cd v10-core
```

### 2. Configure Secrets
```bash
# Criar namespace
kubectl create namespace diyapp-production

# Criar secrets
kubectl create secret generic db-secrets \
  --namespace diyapp-production \
  --from-literal=postgres-password='${PG_PASSWORD}' \
  --from-literal=redis-password='${REDIS_PASSWORD}'

kubectl create secret generic jwt-secrets \
  --namespace diyapp-production \
  --from-literal=jwt-secret='${JWT_SECRET}'

kubectl create secret generic stripe-secrets \
  --namespace diyapp-production \
  --from-literal=stripe-secret-key='${STRIPE_SECRET_KEY}'
```

### 3. Instale Dependências
```bash
# Instalar Istio
istioctl install

### [Sessão Paralela: Compliance]

const winston = require('winston');
const { anonymizeIp } = require('../utils/compliance');

const logger = winston.createLogger({
    format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.timestamp(),
        winston.format.json()
    ),
    transports: [
        new winston.transports.File({ 
            filename: 'logs/access.log',
            maxsize: 5242880, // 5MB
            maxFiles: 5,
            tailable: true
        })
    ]
});

// Middleware de logging com anonimização
const complianceLogger = (req, res, next) => {
    const logData = {
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        method: req.method,
        endpoint: req.url,
        ip: anonymizeIp(req.ip), // Anonimização após 30 dias
        userAgent: req.get('User-Agent'),
        userId: req.user?.id || 'anonymous'
    };
    
    logger.info('API Access', logData);
    
    // Retenção automática - job diário
    if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
        require('../jobs/logRetention').cleanOldLogs();
    }
    
    next();
};

module.exports = { complianceLogger };</code></pre>
